## Combined System: All 60 Skills

With these 40 new skills added to the 26 original skills, CortexBot now has complete coverage of the full autonomous dispatch lifecycle:

```
CARRIER IN                                                    CARRIER PAID
    │                                                              │
    ▼                                                              ▼
[01 Prospect]→[02 Onboard]→[03 FMCSA]→[04 Profile]→[05 Search]→[06 Triage]
                                                                   │
                                                    ←──────────────┘
[10 Book]←[09 Confirm]←[08 Negotiate]←[07 Rate Intel]←[G Voice Call]
   │
   ▼
[11 Packet]→[12 RC Review]→[13 Dispatch]→[14 HOS]→[15 Transit]→[16 Detention]
                                                                    │
                                                     ───────────────┘
[19 Reconcile]←[17 Invoice]←[27 Accessorials]←POD←[Delivery]
   │
   ▼
[Q Fee Collection]→[R Settlement]→[T QuickBooks]→[V 1099]
```

**Parallel systems running always:**
- A (Orchestrator) + B (Queue) + C (Escalation) + D (Event Router) + E (Health)
- 20 (TMS Logging) + 26 (Compliance) + X (Fraud) + L (API Gateway) + N (Email)
- 23 (Weather) + 22 (Fuel) + 21 (Backhaul) + 25 (Performance) + 24 (Broker CRM)

# SKILL: Master Orchestrator
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: System startup. Runs 24/7 as the central intelligence coordinating all workflows.
**Phase**: All phases simultaneously
**Priority**: CRITICAL — without this, every skill runs in isolation

---

## Purpose

The Master Orchestrator is the brain of Cortex Bot. It knows the state of every carrier, every active load, and every pending event at all times. It decides what runs next, prevents race conditions, and ensures nothing falls through the cracks when managing 50+ carriers simultaneously.

---

## Architecture

### LangGraph State Machine

Each active load and carrier has a persistent `LoadState` object tracked in the graph:

```python
from langgraph.graph import StateGraph, END
from typing import TypedDict, List, Optional

class LoadState(TypedDict):
    load_id: str
    carrier_id: str
    status: str          # SEARCHING → BOOKED → DISPATCHED → DELIVERED → PAID
    broker: dict
    rate_agreed: float
    driver: dict
    pickup: dict
    delivery: dict
    documents: list
    financial: dict
    events: list          # Full audit trail
    escalation_flags: list
    skill_outputs: dict
    checkpoint: str
    retry_count: int
    last_updated: str

# Build the master graph
graph = StateGraph(LoadState)

# Register all skill nodes
graph.add_node("search_loads",         load_board_search_agent)
graph.add_node("triage_eligibility",   triage_eligibility_agent)
graph.add_node("rate_intelligence",    rate_intelligence_agent)
graph.add_node("broker_negotiation",   broker_negotiation_agent)
graph.add_node("carrier_confirmation", carrier_confirmation_agent)
graph.add_node("book_load",            load_booking_agent)
graph.add_node("complete_packet",      carrier_packet_agent)
graph.add_node("review_rc",            rate_confirmation_agent)
graph.add_node("dispatch_driver",      driver_dispatch_agent)
graph.add_node("monitor_transit",      transit_monitoring_agent)
graph.add_node("manage_detention",     detention_agent)
graph.add_node("collect_pod",          pod_collection_agent)
graph.add_node("invoice_submit",       invoicing_agent)
graph.add_node("track_payment",        payment_reconciliation_agent)
graph.add_node("human_escalation",     human_escalation_handler)
graph.add_node("emergency_rebroker",   emergency_rebrokering_agent)
```

### Conditional Edge Logic

```python
def route_after_triage(state: LoadState) -> str:
    if state["status"] == "ELIGIBLE":
        return "rate_intelligence"
    elif state["status"] == "NO_LOADS":
        return "search_loads"    # widen search and retry
    elif state["status"] == "ESCALATE":
        return "human_escalation"
    return "search_loads"

def route_after_negotiation(state: LoadState) -> str:
    if state["status"] == "RATE_AGREED":
        return "carrier_confirmation"
    elif state["status"] == "RATE_FAILED":
        return "search_loads"    # try next load
    elif state["status"] == "VOICEMAIL":
        return "search_loads"    # move on, retry later
    return "search_loads"

def route_after_confirmation(state: LoadState) -> str:
    if state["status"] == "CARRIER_CONFIRMED":
        return "book_load"
    elif state["status"] == "CARRIER_REJECTED":
        return "broker_negotiation"  # try different carrier or rate
    elif state["status"] == "TIMEOUT":
        return "search_loads"
    return "search_loads"

def route_after_rc(state: LoadState) -> str:
    if state["status"] == "RC_APPROVED":
        return "dispatch_driver"
    elif state["status"] == "RC_DISCREPANCY":
        return "human_escalation"
    return "human_escalation"

def route_in_transit(state: LoadState) -> str:
    if state["status"] == "DELIVERED":
        return "collect_pod"
    elif state["status"] == "BREAKDOWN":
        return "emergency_rebroker"
    elif state["status"] == "DELAY_CRITICAL":
        return "human_escalation"
    return "monitor_transit"

graph.add_conditional_edges("triage_eligibility",   route_after_triage)
graph.add_conditional_edges("broker_negotiation",   route_after_negotiation)
graph.add_conditional_edges("carrier_confirmation", route_after_confirmation)
graph.add_conditional_edges("review_rc",            route_after_rc)
graph.add_conditional_edges("monitor_transit",      route_in_transit)
```

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — System Startup

On boot:
1. Load all active carrier states from PostgreSQL
2. Load all in-progress load states from LangGraph checkpoints
3. Subscribe to all Redis Stream channels
4. Resume any interrupted workflows from last checkpoint
5. Log: `ORCHESTRATOR_STARTED` with timestamp + carrier count

### Step 2 — Carrier Availability Loop (Runs Every 5 Minutes)

```python
async def carrier_availability_loop():
    while True:
        carriers = await db.get_carriers(status="ACTIVE", has_no_active_load=True)
        
        for carrier in carriers:
            if carrier.last_availability_check > 5_minutes_ago:
                continue
            
            # Check if carrier has submitted availability today
            if not carrier.availability_submitted_today:
                await send_availability_prompt(carrier)
                continue
            
            # Start load search workflow for this carrier
            initial_state = LoadState(
                load_id=generate_load_id(),
                carrier_id=carrier.id,
                status="SEARCHING",
                ...
            )
            
            # Spawn graph execution for this carrier
            await graph.ainvoke(initial_state, config={"thread_id": carrier.id})
        
        await asyncio.sleep(300)  # 5-minute cycle
```

### Step 3 — Event Processing Loop (Runs Continuously)

```python
async def event_processing_loop():
    # Subscribe to all Redis streams
    streams = [
        "cortex:events:carrier",
        "cortex:events:load",
        "cortex:events:transit",
        "cortex:events:documents",
        "cortex:events:payments",
        "cortex:events:alerts",
    ]
    
    while True:
        events = await redis.xread(streams, block=100, count=50)
        
        for stream_name, messages in events:
            for msg_id, event_data in messages:
                await route_event_to_skill(stream_name, event_data)
                await redis.xack(stream_name, "orchestrator", msg_id)
```

### Step 4 — Concurrent Load Management

The orchestrator manages up to 500 concurrent load workflows simultaneously using Python asyncio:

```python
async def route_event_to_skill(stream: str, event: dict):
    event_type = event.get("type")
    entity_id = event.get("entity_id")
    
    routing_table = {
        # GPS events → transit monitoring
        "GPS_UPDATE":          ("monitor_transit", event.get("load_id")),
        # Email received → email parser
        "EMAIL_RECEIVED":      ("email_parsing", None),
        # Payment received → reconciliation
        "PAYMENT_RECEIVED":    ("track_payment", event.get("invoice_id")),
        # Driver message → whatsapp manager
        "WHATSAPP_INBOUND":    ("whatsapp_manager", event.get("carrier_id")),
        # Document uploaded → OCR
        "DOCUMENT_UPLOADED":   ("document_ocr", event.get("doc_id")),
        # Detention clock → detention skill
        "GEOFENCE_ARRIVAL":    ("manage_detention", event.get("load_id")),
        # Compliance expiry → compliance monitor
        "DOC_EXPIRY_ALERT":    ("compliance_monitor", event.get("carrier_id")),
    }
    
    if event_type in routing_table:
        skill_name, target_id = routing_table[event_type]
        await dispatch_skill(skill_name, target_id, event)
```

### Step 5 — Race Condition Prevention

```python
async def dispatch_skill(skill_name: str, entity_id: str, event: dict):
    # Acquire distributed lock before modifying shared state
    lock_key = f"cortex:lock:{entity_id}"
    
    async with redis_lock(lock_key, timeout=30):
        # Load current state
        state = await get_state(entity_id)
        
        # Check if another skill is already running on this entity
        if state.get("running_skill") and state.get("running_skill") != skill_name:
            # Queue it instead of running immediately
            await priority_queue.enqueue(skill_name, entity_id, event, priority="NORMAL")
            return
        
        # Mark skill as running
        state["running_skill"] = skill_name
        await save_state(entity_id, state)
        
        # Execute skill
        result = await run_skill(skill_name, state, event)
        
        # Update state with result
        state.update(result)
        state["running_skill"] = None
        await save_state(entity_id, state)
```

### Step 6 — Checkpoint & Resumability

Every state transition writes a checkpoint to PostgreSQL:

```python
async def save_checkpoint(state: LoadState):
    await db.execute("""
        INSERT INTO load_checkpoints (load_id, state_json, skill_name, timestamp)
        VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())
        ON CONFLICT (load_id) DO UPDATE
        SET state_json = $2, skill_name = $3, timestamp = NOW()
    """, state["load_id"], json.dumps(state), state.get("running_skill"))
```

On system restart, all in-progress loads resume from their last checkpoint automatically.

### Step 7 — Parallel Execution

For each booked load, run these skills concurrently:

```python
async def post_booking_parallel(state: LoadState):
    # Run carrier packet + backhaul planning + fuel optimization simultaneously
    results = await asyncio.gather(
        run_skill("complete_packet", state),
        run_skill("backhaul_planning", state),
        run_skill("fuel_optimization", state),
        return_exceptions=True
    )
    return merge_results(results)

async def transit_parallel(state: LoadState):
    # Run all transit monitors simultaneously
    results = await asyncio.gather(
        run_skill("gps_monitor", state),
        run_skill("hos_compliance", state),
        run_skill("weather_monitor", state),
        run_skill("detention_clock", state),
        run_skill("check_call_manager", state),
        return_exceptions=True
    )
    return merge_results(results)
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Skill throws exception | Catch, log to Sentry, retry up to 3x with backoff |
| State corruption detected | Load last valid checkpoint; flag for review |
| Redis connection lost | Switch to in-memory queue; reconnect with backoff |
| Database unavailable | Cache writes locally; sync on reconnect |
| Skill timeout (>120s) | Kill skill, log SKILL_TIMEOUT, resume from last checkpoint |
| All retries exhausted | Route to human-escalation-protocol (Skill C) |
| 10+ escalations in 1 hour | Page on-call operator immediately |

skill_id: "B-priority-queue-manager"
name: "Priority Queue Manager"
version: "1.0.0"
phase: 0
priority: critical
trigger: "Runs as a background service. Called whenever multiple events compete for the same carrier or load resource."
inputs:
  - incoming_events: "all events from Redis Streams requiring skill execution"
  - active_skill_slots: "how many skills are currently executing"
  - carrier_states: "current priority level per carrier"
  - load_urgency_scores: "calculated urgency for each active load"
outputs:
  - execution_order: "ranked queue of skills to run"
  - preemption_decisions: "lower-priority skills paused for critical ones"
  - queue_metrics: "depth, wait times, throughput"
integrations:
  - BullMQ (Redis-backed job queue)
  - Redis Streams
  - PostgreSQL
  - master-orchestrator (skill A)
depends_on: ["A-master-orchestrator"]
triggers_next: ["whichever skill is next in queue"]
tags: [queue, priority, scheduling, concurrency, bullmq, coordination]
---

# SKILL: Priority Queue Manager
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Continuous — governs all skill execution order.
**Phase**: All phases
**Priority**: CRITICAL

---

## Purpose

When 50 carriers are active and events fire simultaneously (carrier confirms load WHILE detention clock starts WHILE RC arrives WHILE driver goes missing), this skill decides what gets CPU time first. Wrong prioritization = missed bookings, late responses, and lost revenue.

---

## Priority Tiers

| Priority | Score | Event Type | Max Wait Time |
|----------|-------|-----------|---------------|
| P0 — Emergency | 1000 | Driver breakdown, cargo theft, HOS violation imminent | 0s — preempt everything |
| P1 — Critical | 800 | Broker holding for MC#, carrier confirmation loop, RC discrepancy | <5s |
| P2 — High | 600 | New load opportunity, detention start, POD collection, invoice due | <30s |
| P3 — Medium | 400 | Check-call due, backhaul search, compliance alert | <2min |
| P4 — Normal | 200 | Performance scoring, broker CRM update, fuel optimization | <10min |
| P5 — Batch | 100 | Weekly reports, 1099 generation, analytics | Next batch window |

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Queue Architecture (BullMQ)

```javascript
// BullMQ queue setup (Node.js)
import { Queue, Worker, QueueScheduler } from 'bullmq';
import Redis from 'ioredis';

const connection = new Redis({ host: process.env.REDIS_HOST });

// Separate queues per priority tier
const queues = {
  emergency: new Queue('cortex:emergency', { connection }),
  critical:  new Queue('cortex:critical',  { connection }),
  high:      new Queue('cortex:high',      { connection }),
  medium:    new Queue('cortex:medium',    { connection }),
  normal:    new Queue('cortex:normal',    { connection }),
  batch:     new Queue('cortex:batch',     { connection }),
};

// Workers with concurrency limits per tier
const workers = {
  emergency: new Worker('cortex:emergency', processJob, { connection, concurrency: 50 }),
  critical:  new Worker('cortex:critical',  processJob, { connection, concurrency: 30 }),
  high:      new Worker('cortex:high',      processJob, { connection, concurrency: 20 }),
  medium:    new Worker('cortex:medium',    processJob, { connection, concurrency: 10 }),
  normal:    new Worker('cortex:normal',    processJob, { connection, concurrency: 5  }),
  batch:     new Worker('cortex:batch',     processJob, { connection, concurrency: 2  }),
};
```

### Step 2 — Event Priority Assignment

```python
def assign_priority(event: dict) -> int:
    event_type = event.get("type")
    
    # P0 — Emergency (immediate preemption)
    p0_events = {
        "BREAKDOWN_REPORTED",
        "CARGO_THEFT_DETECTED",
        "HOS_LIMIT_REACHED",
        "DRIVER_UNRESPONSIVE_3X",
        "AUTHORITY_LAPSED_MID_DISPATCH",
        "EMERGENCY_REBROKER_NEEDED",
    }
    if event_type in p0_events:
        return 1000

    # P1 — Critical (broker waiting, time-sensitive)
    p1_events = {
        "BROKER_HOLDING_FOR_MC",
        "CARRIER_CONFIRMATION_TIMEOUT_60S",
        "RC_DISCREPANCY_FOUND",
        "FACTORING_SUBMISSION_DUE",
        "PAYMENT_OVERDUE_14_DAYS",
    }
    if event_type in p1_events:
        return 800
    
    # P2 — High (revenue-generating, time-sensitive)
    p2_events = {
        "NEW_LOAD_FOUND",
        "GEOFENCE_ARRIVAL",
        "DETENTION_CLOCK_START",
        "DELIVERY_CONFIRMED",
        "POD_RECEIVED",
        "INVOICE_READY",
    }
    if event_type in p2_events:
        return 600
    
    # P3 — Medium
    p3_events = {
        "CHECK_CALL_DUE",
        "COMPLIANCE_EXPIRY_7_DAYS",
        "BACKHAUL_SEARCH_TRIGGER",
        "WEATHER_WARNING",
    }
    if event_type in p3_events:
        return 400
    
    # Default to Normal
    return 200

def enqueue_skill(skill_name: str, entity_id: str, event: dict):
    priority = assign_priority(event)
    queue_name = priority_to_queue(priority)
    
    job = {
        "skill": skill_name,
        "entity_id": entity_id,
        "event": event,
        "enqueued_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "priority": priority,
    }
    
    queues[queue_name].add(f"{skill_name}:{entity_id}", job, {
        "priority": priority,
        "attempts": 3,
        "backoff": {"type": "exponential", "delay": 1000},
        "removeOnComplete": 100,
        "removeOnFail": 50,
    })
```

### Step 3 — Preemption Logic

When a P0 event fires while P4 skills are running:

```python
async def handle_preemption(emergency_event: dict):
    carrier_id = emergency_event.get("carrier_id")
    
    # Find all running skills for this carrier
    running_skills = await get_running_skills(carrier_id)
    
    for skill in running_skills:
        if skill.priority < 800:
            # Checkpoint current state
            await save_checkpoint(skill.state)
            
            # Pause the skill
            await skill.pause()
            
            # Log preemption
            log(f"PREEMPTED {skill.name} for emergency on {carrier_id}")
    
    # Execute emergency skill immediately
    await run_emergency_skill(emergency_event)
    
    # Resume paused skills
    for skill in running_skills:
        await skill.resume()
```

### Step 4 — Starvation Prevention

Low-priority jobs should not wait indefinitely:

```python
async def prevent_starvation():
    """Boost priority of jobs waiting too long"""
    while True:
        # Check all queued jobs
        all_jobs = await get_all_queued_jobs()
        
        for job in all_jobs:
            wait_time = (datetime.utcnow() - job.enqueued_at).seconds
            
            # Boost priority based on wait time
            if job.priority == 200 and wait_time > 600:   # 10 min
                await boost_priority(job, 400)
            elif job.priority == 400 and wait_time > 300:  # 5 min
                await boost_priority(job, 600)
        
        await asyncio.sleep(60)
```

### Step 5 — Queue Health Monitoring

```python
async def monitor_queue_health():
    metrics = {}
    
    for queue_name, queue in queues.items():
        waiting = await queue.getWaitingCount()
        active = await queue.getActiveCount()
        failed = await queue.getFailedCount()
        
        metrics[queue_name] = {
            "waiting": waiting,
            "active": active,
            "failed": failed,
            "throughput_per_min": await get_throughput(queue_name),
        }
        
        # Alert if critical queue is backing up
        if queue_name == "critical" and waiting > 50:
            await send_alert("CRITICAL QUEUE BACKLOG", f"{waiting} jobs waiting in critical queue")
        
        if queue_name == "emergency" and waiting > 5:
            await page_oncall("EMERGENCY QUEUE BACKLOG")
    
    return metrics
```

---

## Queue Depth Thresholds

| Queue | Warning | Critical | Action |
|-------|---------|---------|--------|
| Emergency | >2 | >5 | Page on-call immediately |
| Critical | >20 | >50 | Alert Slack + scale workers |
| High | >100 | >200 | Alert Slack |
| Medium | >500 | >1000 | Log warning |
| Batch | >5000 | N/A | Log info |

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Job fails 3 times | Move to dead-letter queue; alert dashboard |
| Worker crashes | BullMQ auto-restarts; jobs requeue automatically |
| Redis unavailable | In-memory fallback queue; sync on reconnect |
| Queue depth alarm | Auto-scale worker count via ECS |

# SKILL: Human Escalation Protocol
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Any situation the bot cannot autonomously resolve.
**Phase**: All phases
**Priority**: CRITICAL — this is the safety net for every automated decision

---

## Purpose

Define exactly when and how the bot hands off to a human, ensuring no load falls through the cracks and every escalation reaches the right person within the SLA window.

---

## Escalation Scenarios

### Scenario Catalog

| ID | Trigger | Urgency | SLA | Human Action Needed |
|----|---------|---------|-----|-------------------|
| E01 | AI call confidence <0.75 after 2 attempts | P1 | 5 min | Human calls broker directly |
| E02 | RC has discrepancy bot cannot resolve | P1 | 10 min | Review RC, call broker |
| E03 | Carrier breakdown mid-load | P0 | 2 min | Authorize emergency rebroker |
| E04 | Cargo damage or theft reported | P0 | 2 min | Initiate claims protocol |
| E05 | Broker disputes invoice >$500 | P1 | 30 min | Review dispute, negotiate |
| E06 | Driver unresponsive >2 hours | P0 | 5 min | Attempt contact, assess load risk |
| E07 | FMCSA authority lapsed mid-dispatch | P0 | 2 min | Pull truck, notify broker |
| E08 | Broker credit score drops below 40 | P1 | 15 min | Decide to continue or pull carrier |
| E09 | HOS violation unavoidable | P0 | 5 min | Coordinate reset, notify broker |
| E10 | Carrier wants to quit mid-load | P0 | 5 min | Negotiate or emergency rebroker |
| E11 | Weather forces indefinite hold | P1 | 15 min | Authorize hold cost, notify shipper |
| E12 | Lumper refuses to release freight | P1 | 10 min | Authorize payment or negotiate |
| E13 | Broker won't send RC for >1 hour | P1 | 20 min | Call broker, confirm or cancel |
| E14 | Factoring company rejects advance | P1 | 30 min | Troubleshoot or direct pay |
| E15 | Collections required >$1000 | P2 | 1 day | Review and authorize collections action |
| E16 | New carrier onboarding edge case | P2 | 2 hours | Manual document review |
| E17 | Double brokering suspected | P0 | 5 min | Do not proceed; investigate |
| E18 | Driver reports wrong commodity loaded | P1 | 10 min | Coordinate with broker and shipper |

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Assess Escalation Urgency

```python
def assess_escalation(reason_code: str, context: dict) -> dict:
    escalation_config = ESCALATION_SCENARIOS[reason_code]
    
    urgency = escalation_config["urgency"]
    sla_minutes = escalation_config["sla_minutes"]
    
    # Calculate deadline
    deadline = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=sla_minutes)
    
    # Choose notification channels based on urgency
    channels = {
        "P0": ["pagerduty", "sms", "whatsapp", "dashboard"],
        "P1": ["sms", "whatsapp", "dashboard"],
        "P2": ["dashboard", "slack"],
    }.get(urgency, ["dashboard"])
    
    return {
        "reason": reason_code,
        "urgency": urgency,
        "deadline": deadline.isoformat(),
        "channels": channels,
        "context": context,
    }
```

### Step 2 — Create Escalation Ticket

```python
def create_escalation_ticket(escalation: dict) -> dict:
    ticket = {
        "ticket_id": f"ESC-{datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S')}",
        "created_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "urgency": escalation["urgency"],
        "deadline": escalation["deadline"],
        "reason": escalation["reason"],
        "reason_description": ESCALATION_SCENARIOS[escalation["reason"]]["description"],
        "load_id": escalation["context"].get("load_id"),
        "carrier_id": escalation["context"].get("carrier_id"),
        "carrier_name": escalation["context"].get("carrier_name"),
        "broker_name": escalation["context"].get("broker_name"),
        "current_status": escalation["context"].get("status"),
        "attempted_actions": escalation["context"].get("attempted_actions", []),
        "recommended_actions": ESCALATION_SCENARIOS[escalation["reason"]]["recommended_actions"],
        "context_snapshot": escalation["context"],
        "status": "OPEN",
    }
    
    # Save to database
    db.insert("escalations", ticket)
    return ticket
```

### Step 3 — Multi-Channel Alert Dispatch

**PagerDuty (P0 only):**
```python
pagerduty.create_incident(
    title=f"[P0] {ticket['reason_description']}",
    body=f"Load: {ticket['load_id']} | Carrier: {ticket['carrier_name']} | Deadline: {ticket['deadline']}",
    severity="critical",
    escalation_policy="on-call-dispatcher",
)
```

**SMS to On-Call Operator:**
```
🚨 P0 ESCALATION — CORTEX BOT
Ticket: ESC-20260320-001
Issue: [Reason Description]
Load: [Load ID] | Carrier: [Name]
Deadline: [Time]
Action: [What needs to happen]
Dashboard: https://app.cortexbot.com/escalations/ESC-001
```

**WhatsApp to On-Call:**
```
🚨 HUMAN ACTION NEEDED
[Full context including what bot already tried]
[Recommended next steps]
[One-tap response options: RESOLVED ✅ | CALL ME 📞 | ESCALATE ⬆️]
```

**Dashboard Notification:**
- New ticket appears in escalation queue with countdown timer
- Full context panel with all relevant load/carrier data
- Action buttons: RESOLVE | REASSIGN | SNOOZE (5 min)
- Countdown timer shows SLA deadline

### Step 4 — Fallback Action (If Human Doesn't Respond in Time)

If no acknowledgement within SLA × 1.5:

```python
async def execute_fallback(ticket: dict):
    reason = ticket["reason"]
    
    fallback_actions = {
        "E01": lambda: release_load_and_try_next(),           # Call failed — try email
        "E02": lambda: hold_dispatch_pending_review(),         # Don't sign bad RC
        "E03": lambda: initiate_emergency_rebrokering(),       # Auto-rebroker
        "E06": lambda: call_emergency_contact_on_file(),       # Call next contact
        "E07": lambda: suspend_carrier_and_notify_broker(),    # Legal — must suspend
        "E17": lambda: cancel_load_and_flag_broker(),          # Fraud risk — don't proceed
    }
    
    fallback = fallback_actions.get(reason)
    if fallback:
        result = await fallback()
        log(f"FALLBACK_EXECUTED for {reason}: {result}")
    
    # Re-alert with higher urgency
    await send_alert(
        f"FALLBACK TRIGGERED — {reason}",
        f"No human response within SLA. Fallback action executed: {result}",
        urgency="P0",
    )
```

### Step 5 — Human Resolution Recording

When operator marks ticket resolved in dashboard:

```python
def record_resolution(ticket_id: str, resolution: dict):
    # Update ticket
    db.update("escalations", ticket_id, {
        "status": "RESOLVED",
        "resolved_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "resolved_by": resolution["operator_id"],
        "resolution_action": resolution["action_taken"],
        "resolution_notes": resolution["notes"],
        "resume_instruction": resolution.get("resume_instruction"),
    })
    
    # Resume the paused workflow
    if resolution.get("resume_instruction"):
        orchestrator.resume_workflow(
            entity_id=ticket["load_id"] or ticket["carrier_id"],
            instruction=resolution["resume_instruction"],
        )
    
    # Log for training
    log_escalation_outcome(ticket_id, resolution)
```

- Total escalations per week by type
- Average resolution time per scenario type
- Escalations that required fallback action (bot failed to get human attention)
- Most common escalation types → candidates for autonomous resolution improvement
- Cost per escalation (operator time × hourly rate)

|-----------|--------|

| On-call not responding | Escalate to secondary operator |
| No operators available | Execute conservative fallback for P0/P1 |
| Dashboard inaccessible | Send full context via SMS/email |

# SKILL: Event Router
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Every incoming event from every external channel.
**Phase**: All — runs as an always-on service
**Priority**: CRITICAL — without this, nothing responds to the real world

---

## Purpose

Be the single intake point for all external signals. Route each event to exactly the right skill. A mis-routed event means a missed detention claim, a missed load, or a missed payment.

---

## Routing Table

### Email Events

```python
EMAIL_ROUTING_RULES = [
    # Subject patterns → skill
    (r"rate confirmation|rate con|RC#",          "rate_confirmation_review"),
    (r"carrier packet|setup packet|carrier setup","carrier_packet_completion"),
    (r"invoice|payment|remittance|check",         "payment_reconciliation"),
    (r"detention|layover|accessorial",            "accessorials_tracking"),
    (r"claim|damage|shortage|dispute",            "freight_claims_management"),
    (r"authority|fmcsa|mc number",               "fmcsa_verification"),
    (r"insurance|coi|certificate",               "compliance_monitoring"),
    (r"load tender|204|load offer",              "edi_integration"),
    (r"out of service|breakdown|emergency",       "human_escalation_protocol"),
    # Default: classify with LLM if no pattern matches
    (r".*",                                       "email_parsing_automation"),
]
```

### SMS/WhatsApp Events

```python
def route_driver_message(message: str, sender_id: str) -> str:
    # Detect document image attachment
    if message.get("media_url"):
        if is_document_photo(message["media_url"]):
            return "document_ocr_intelligence"
    
    text = message["body"].lower().strip()
    
    # Keyword routing
    keywords = {
        "confirmed|yes|go|ok|good": "carrier_confirmation_loop",
        "no|can't|pass|skip":       "carrier_confirmation_loop",
        "at pickup|arrived|here":   "in_transit_monitoring",
        "loaded|rolling|departed":  "in_transit_monitoring",
        "delivered|empty|done":     "pod_invoicing_factoring",
        "breakdown|broke down|accident": "emergency_rebrokering",
        "lumper|need code|auth":    "detention_layover_management",
        "delay|late|traffic":       "in_transit_monitoring",
        "help|call me|emergency":   "human_escalation_protocol",
    }
    
    for pattern, skill in keywords.items():
        if any(kw in text for kw in pattern.split("|")):
            return skill
    
    # LLM classification for ambiguous messages
    return classify_with_llm(message["body"])
```

### Webhook Events

```python
WEBHOOK_ROUTING = {
    # Bland AI
    "bland_ai.call_completed":    "ai_voice_broker_calling",
    "bland_ai.voicemail_left":    "voicemail_afterhours_handler",
    
    # ELD providers
    "samsara.gps_update":         "in_transit_monitoring",
```


---

## LLM Classification (For Ambiguous Events)

When no rule matches, use a fast LLM call to classify:

```python
async def classify_with_llm(content: str, source: str) -> str:
    response = await llm.complete(
        model="gpt-4o-mini",  # fast + cheap for classification
        system="""You are an event router for a truck dispatch system.
        Classify the incoming message into exactly ONE of these skills:
        load_board_search, broker_negotiation, carrier_confirmation_loop,
        rate_confirmation_review, carrier_packet_completion, driver_dispatch,
        in_transit_monitoring, detention_layover_management, pod_invoicing_factoring,
        payment_reconciliation, compliance_monitoring, human_escalation_protocol,
        email_parsing_automation, freight_claims_management, emergency_rebrokering.
        Reply with ONLY the skill name, nothing else.""",
        user=f"Source: {source}\nContent: {content[:500]}",
        max_tokens=30,
    )
    
    skill = response.strip()
    confidence = 0.7  # LLM classification confidence
    
    log(f"LLM_ROUTED: {content[:50]}... → {skill} ({confidence})")
    return skill, confidence
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Unknown event type | Route to email_parsing_automation for further analysis |
| LLM classification fails | Route to human_escalation_protocol |
| Routing loop detected | Break loop and log; route to human |
| Event payload malformed | Log raw event; alert but don't crash |
| High event volume spike | Enable rate limiting; queue overflow to batch |

# SKILL: System Health Monitor
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Continuous — every 60 seconds health check.
**Phase**: All
**Priority**: HIGH

---

## Purpose

Know about system degradation before it kills a load. When DAT API slows down during morning search, when Bland AI has elevated latency during a negotiation, when the database is overloaded — catch it immediately and route around it.

---

## Health Check Matrix

### External API Health

```python
async def check_all_api_health():
    apis = [
        {"name": "DAT_Load_Board",    "url": "https://api.dat.com/health",        "sla_ms": 500,  "critical": True},
        {"name": "Bland_AI_Calling",  "url": "https://api.bland.ai/health",       "sla_ms": 300,  "critical": True},
        {"name": "FMCSA_SAFER",       "url": "https://safer.fmcsa.dot.gov",       "sla_ms": 2000, "critical": True},
        {"name": "Twilio_SMS",        "url": "https://api.twilio.com/health",     "sla_ms": 500,  "critical": True},
        {"name": "Samsara_ELD",       "url": "https://api.samsara.com/v1/health", "sla_ms": 1000, "critical": False},
        {"name": "Motive_ELD",        "url": "https://api.keeptruckin.com/health","sla_ms": 1000, "critical": False},
        {"name": "SendGrid_Email",    "url": "https://api.sendgrid.com/health",   "sla_ms": 500,  "critical": True},
        {"name": "AWS_S3",            "url": "https://s3.amazonaws.com",          "sla_ms": 200,  "critical": True},
        {"name": "Truckstop",         "url": "https://api.truckstop.com/health",  "sla_ms": 500,  "critical": False},
        {"name": "QuickBooks",        "url": "https://oauth.platform.intuit.com", "sla_ms": 1000, "critical": False},
    ]
    
    results = await asyncio.gather(*[check_api(api) for api in apis])
    return results

async def check_api(api: dict) -> dict:
    start = time.time()
    try:
        response = await http.get(api["url"], timeout=5)
        latency_ms = (time.time() - start) * 1000
        
        return {
            "name": api["name"],
            "status": "UP" if response.status_code < 400 else "DEGRADED",
            "latency_ms": latency_ms,
            "above_sla": latency_ms > api["sla_ms"],
            "critical": api["critical"],
        }
    except Exception as e:
        return {
            "name": api["name"],
            "status": "DOWN",
            "error": str(e),
            "critical": api["critical"],
        }
```

### Fallback Routing on API Failure

```python
FALLBACK_ROUTES = {
    "DAT_Load_Board":   "Truckstop",           # Secondary load board
    "Bland_AI_Calling": "human_escalation",    # Human makes the call
    "Samsara_ELD":      "Motive_ELD",          # Alternative ELD
    "Motive_ELD":       "manual_check_call",   # Revert to manual check-calls
    "SendGrid_Email":   "Twilio_SMS",          # SMS as fallback
    "FMCSA_SAFER":      "cached_fmcsa_data",   # Use last known status
}
```

## Alerting Thresholds

| Metric | Warning | Critical | Action |
|--------|---------|---------|--------|
| API error rate | >2% | >5% | Switch to fallback; alert |
| API latency | >2× SLA | >5× SLA | Circuit breaker; fallback |
| Queue depth (critical) | >50 | >100 | Scale workers; alert |
| DB query time | >500ms | >2000ms | Alert DBA; read replica |
| LLM token budget exceeded | >80% | >95% | Switch to cheaper model |
| Active load count drop | >20% in 1hr | >40% in 1hr | Investigate; alert |

# SKILL: A/B Testing Framework
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Silently assigns test variants; evaluates weekly.
**Phase**: All
**Priority**: MEDIUM

---

## Purpose

Continuously improve negotiation scripts, carrier outreach messages, and dispatch templates through controlled experiments. Over time, A/B testing is the primary mechanism for increasing average CPM achieved.

---

## Active Experiment Types

### Experiment 1 — Negotiation Opening Lines

```python
EXPERIMENTS = {
    "negotiation_opening": {
        "description": "Which opening line achieves highest rate",
        "variants": {
            "A": "Based on current DAT data, this lane is averaging $X.XX...",
            "B": "We have equipment positioned specifically for this lane...",
            "C": "Given current market tightness in [origin], we're targeting...",
        },
        "metric": "avg_rate_vs_market",
        "sample_size": 100,
        "min_significance": 0.95,
    },
    
    "carrier_outreach_channel": {
        "description": "WhatsApp vs SMS vs call for initial contact",
        "variants": {
            "A": "whatsapp_first",
            "B": "sms_first",
            "C": "call_first",
        },
        "metric": "response_rate_within_60s",
        "sample_size": 200,
    },
    
    "detention_notice_timing": {
        "description": "Alert broker at 1:45 vs 1:30 vs 2:00 (at clock start)",
        "variants": {
            "A": "15_min_before",
            "B": "30_min_before",
            "C": "at_clock_start",
        },
        "metric": "detention_claim_payment_rate",
        "sample_size": 150,
    },
}
```

### Assignment Logic

```python
def assign_variant(experiment_name: str, entity_id: str) -> str:
    # Deterministic assignment based on entity_id hash
    # Ensures same carrier/load always gets same variant
    hash_val = int(hashlib.md5(f"{experiment_name}:{entity_id}".encode()).hexdigest(), 16)
    variants = list(EXPERIMENTS[experiment_name]["variants"].keys())
    variant = variants[hash_val % len(variants)]
    
    # Log assignment
    db.insert("experiment_assignments", {
        "experiment": experiment_name,
        "entity_id": entity_id,
        "variant": variant,
        "assigned_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
    })
    
    return variant
```

### Results Analysis (Weekly)

```python
def analyze_experiment(experiment_name: str) -> dict:
    results = db.query("""
        SELECT variant, 
               COUNT(*) as n,
               AVG(metric_value) as mean,
               STDDEV(metric_value) as std
        FROM experiment_results
        WHERE experiment = $1
        AND assigned_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '30 days'
        GROUP BY variant
    """, experiment_name)
    
    # Statistical significance test (t-test between variants)
    winner = None
    for variant_a, variant_b in combinations(results, 2):
        t_stat, p_value = stats.ttest_ind_from_stats(
            variant_a["mean"], variant_a["std"], variant_a["n"],
            variant_b["mean"], variant_b["std"], variant_b["n"],
        )
        
        if p_value < 0.05:  # 95% confidence
            winner = variant_a if variant_a["mean"] > variant_b["mean"] else variant_b
    
    if winner:
        promote_to_production(experiment_name, winner["variant"])
    
    return {"experiment": experiment_name, "winner": winner, "results": results}
```

# SKILL: AI Voice Broker Calling
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Eligible load identified; rate brief prepared; ready to call broker.
**Phase**: 6–7 (Broker Contact + Rate Negotiation)
**Priority**: CRITICAL — this IS the automation. Without this, a human still calls.

---

## Purpose

Make actual phone calls to freight brokers, gather load details, and negotiate rates — autonomously, in real time, sounding like a professional human dispatcher. This is what makes Cortex Bot fully autonomous rather than just a load-tracking tool.

---

## Platform: Bland AI

Bland AI is selected because:
- ~800ms response latency (human-quality conversation pace)
- Native mid-call function calls (inject live DAT rates during negotiation)
- Cross-call memory (remembers this broker from prior calls)
- Visual conversation pathway builder
- $0.09/min transparent pricing
- RBAC + call recording + audit logs

---

## Conversation Pathway Design

### Stage 1 — Opening

```
AI Dispatcher: "Hi, this is [Dispatcher Name] calling on behalf of [Carrier Company] — 
we have a 53-foot dry van available in [origin city] today. I'm reaching out about 
the [origin → destination] load you have posted on DAT, reference [REF#]. 
Is now a good time to go over the details?"

PATHWAY BRANCHES:
  → "Yes / Sure / Go ahead" → Stage 2 (Detail Gathering)
  → "It's covered" → CALL_OUTCOME: LOAD_COVERED, end call gracefully
  → "Call back later" → Schedule callback in 30 min, end call
  → "Not interested" → CALL_OUTCOME: NOT_INTERESTED, end call
  → Hung up / No answer → CALL_OUTCOME: NO_ANSWER
```

### Stage 2 — Detail Gathering (20+ fields)

```python
DETAIL_GATHERING_QUESTIONS = [
    {
        "field": "pickup_address",
        "question": "Can you give me the full pickup address including city and zip?",
        "validation": lambda v: len(v) > 10,
    },
    {
        "field": "pickup_appointment",
        "question": "And what's the pickup appointment — specific time or first come first serve?",
    },
    {
        "field": "delivery_address",
        "question": "Perfect. And the delivery address?",
    },
    {
        "field": "delivery_appointment",
        "question": "Delivery appointment or FCFS window?",
    },
    {
        "field": "commodity",
        "question": "What's the commodity?",
    },
    {
        "field": "weight",
        "question": "And the weight — roughly how many pounds?",
    },
    {
        "field": "load_type",
        "question": "Is this a live load or drop and hook?",
    },
    {
        "field": "lumper",
        "question": "Any lumper required at delivery? If so, broker-paid or carrier-paid?",
    },
    {
        "field": "detention_terms",
        "question": "What are the detention terms — how many free hours before it starts billing?",
    },
    {
        "field": "tonu",
        "question": "If the load gets cancelled after we're dispatched, what's the TONU amount?",
    },
    {
        "field": "tracking",
        "question": "What tracking do you require — Macropoint, FourKites, or your own system?",
    },
    {
        "field": "payment_terms",
        "question": "And payment terms — Net 15, Net 30? Any quick-pay option?",
    },
    {
        "field": "factoring_allowed",
        "question": "Do you work with factoring companies?",
    },
]
```

### Stage 3 — Rate Negotiation

```python
# Bland AI mid-call webhook to get live market data
BLAND_AI_FUNCTION = {
    "name": "get_negotiation_data",
    "description": "Get live DAT rate and negotiation strategy for this lane",
    "parameters": {
        "origin_city": "string",
        "destination_city": "string",
        "equipment": "string",
    },
    "webhook_url": "https://api.cortexbot.com/bland/rate-data",
    "response_timeout_ms": 200,
}

# Cortex Bot responds in <200ms with:
def get_negotiation_data(origin: str, destination: str, equipment: str) -> dict:
    rate_brief = rate_intelligence.get_brief(origin, destination, equipment)
    
    return {
        "market_rate_7day": rate_brief.market_rate_7day,
        "load_to_truck_ratio": rate_brief.load_to_truck_ratio,
        "anchor_rate": rate_brief.anchor_rate,
        "counter_rate": rate_brief.counter_rate,
        "walk_away_rate": rate_brief.walk_away_rate,
        "talking_points": rate_brief.talking_points,
        "market_condition": rate_brief.market_condition,
    }
```

**Negotiation Script — Bland AI Pathway:**

```
# After gathering all details, fetch live rate data via function call

AI Dispatcher: "Based on current market data — DAT is showing this lane 
averaging $[market_rate] this week with a [load_to_truck_ratio] load-to-truck 
ratio — so market's [tight/balanced/loose]. For this load we'd be looking 
at around [$anchor_rate] all-in. What can you do?"

BROKER RESPONSE BRANCHES:
  → Accepts anchor: → RATE_AGREED, proceed to Stage 4
  → Counter between anchor and counter_rate:
      AI: "That works — let me confirm with my driver. Give me 60 seconds."
      → Proceed to Stage 4 (Hold)
  → Counter at or above walk_away_rate:
      AI: "That's a little tight for my carrier. Could we get to [$counter_rate]? 
           That accounts for the [X] miles of deadhead from [origin]."
      → If yes: RATE_AGREED
      → If no and above floor: AI accepts
      → If below floor: "I don't think I can make this work at that rate 
           given current market. If the rate changes, I'll reach back out. 
           Appreciate your time."
  → Far below walk_away_rate: Decline gracefully, end call
```

### Stage 4 — Hold & Carrier Confirmation

```
AI Dispatcher: "Let me put you on a quick hold — 60 seconds — 
while I confirm with my driver."

[Plays hold music]
[Simultaneously sends WhatsApp to carrier via skill 09]
[Waits for carrier response — max 90 seconds]

IF CARRIER CONFIRMS:
AI Dispatcher: "Great, we're confirmed. Book it. 
Our MC number is [MC#]. Please send the carrier packet and rate 
confirmation to [email]. My driver's name is [First Name], 
cell [phone]. We're set for [pickup date/time]."
→ CALL_OUTCOME: BOOKED

IF CARRIER REJECTS:
AI Dispatcher: "I appreciate your time — I need to check on a couple 
more loads first. If I don't find a better fit, I'll give you a call back. 
Thanks!"
→ CALL_OUTCOME: CARRIER_REJECTED
```

### Stage 5 — Close or Release

```
BOOK IT flow:
AI Dispatcher: "Perfect. Just to confirm — $[rate] all-in, 
[pickup date/time], [delivery date/time], detention starts 
at 2 hours free then $[rate]/hour, TONU of $[amount] 
if cancelled after dispatch. That all look right on your end? 
... Great. We'll get the paperwork back to you quickly. 
Have a good one!"

RELEASE flow:
AI Dispatcher: "I appreciate it — if anything comes up 
on my end I'll be in touch. Have a good one!"
```

---

## Bland AI Integration Code

```python
import requests

async def initiate_broker_call(load_candidate: dict, rate_brief: dict) -> dict:
    
    payload = {
        "phone_number": load_candidate["broker_phone"],
        "from_number": CORTEX_BOT_CALLER_ID,
        "task": build_call_task(load_candidate, rate_brief),
        "voice": "nat",                    # Professional, human-sounding voice
        "background_track": "office-ambience",  # Subtle office noise for realism
        "model": "enhanced",
        "language": "en-US",
        "max_duration": 600,               # 10-minute max call
        "record": True,
        "webhook": "https://api.cortexbot.com/webhooks/bland/call-complete",
        "tools": [BLAND_AI_FUNCTION],       # Live rate data injection
        "metadata": {
            "load_id": load_candidate["load_id"],
            "carrier_id": load_candidate["carrier_id"],
            "rate_brief": rate_brief,
        },
    }
    
    response = requests.post(
        "https://api.bland.ai/v1/calls",
        headers={"authorization": BLAND_AI_API_KEY},
        json=payload,
    )
    
    call_id = response.json()["call_id"]
    
    # Log call initiated
    await tms.log("BROKER_CALL_INITIATED", {
        "call_id": call_id,
        "broker_phone": load_candidate["broker_phone"],
        "load_id": load_candidate["load_id"],
    })
    
    return {"call_id": call_id, "status": "INITIATED"}

def build_call_task(load: dict, rate: dict) -> str:
    return f"""
    You are a professional truck dispatcher calling about a freight load.
    
    LOAD DETAILS:
    - Reference: {load['ref_number']}
    - Origin: {load['origin_city']}, {load['origin_state']}
    - Destination: {load['dest_city']}, {load['dest_state']}
    - Equipment: {load['equipment_type']}
    - Pickup: {load['pickup_date']}
    
    NEGOTIATION PARAMETERS:
    - Anchor rate: ${rate['anchor_rate']}/mile
    - Walk-away minimum: ${rate['walk_away_rate']}/mile  
    - Market talking points: {rate['talking_points']}
    
    STYLE: Professional, confident, conversational. Sound like an experienced human dispatcher.
    Use natural speech — occasional "um" or "let me check that" is fine.
    Never reveal you are an AI. If directly asked, say you're with [Carrier Company] dispatch.
    
    GOAL: Get the load booked at the highest achievable rate with all accessorials locked.
    """
```

---

## Call Outcome Processing

```python
async def process_call_completion(webhook_data: dict):
    call_id = webhook_data["call_id"]
    transcript = webhook_data["transcript"]
    recording_url = webhook_data["recording_url"]
    
    # Extract structured data from transcript using LLM
    extraction = await extract_call_data(transcript)
    
    outcome = extraction["outcome"]  # BOOKED / RATE_TOO_LOW / NO_ANSWER / etc.
    
    if outcome == "BOOKED":
        # Trigger carrier confirmation loop
        await carrier_confirmation_loop.start(
            load_id=extraction["load_id"],
            agreed_rate=extraction["agreed_rate"],
            accessorials=extraction["locked_accessorials"],
        )
    elif outcome in ["NO_ANSWER", "VOICEMAIL"]:
        # Hand off to voicemail handler
        await voicemail_handler.process(call_id, extraction)
    
    # Log everything
    await tms.log("BROKER_CALL_COMPLETED", {
        "call_id": call_id,
        "outcome": outcome,
        "agreed_rate": extraction.get("agreed_rate"),
        "duration_seconds": webhook_data["duration"],
        "recording_url": recording_url,
        "transcript": transcript,
    })
```

---

## Call Quality Standards

- Average call duration target: 3–6 minutes
- Rate achievement target: >105% of DAT market average
- Successful booking rate target: >25% of calls (industry avg ~15–20%)
- Broker complaint rate target: <1%
- Natural speech quality: scored weekly by sampling 10 random calls

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Bland AI API unavailable | Route to human escalation for manual call |
| Call connects but broker very hostile | Gracefully end call; flag broker in CRM |
| Broker asks for supervisor | Route to human escalation immediately |
| Rate extracted incorrectly from transcript | Flag for human review; don't book |
| Carrier changes mind after call books | Emergency rebroker protocol |

# SKILL: Voicemail & After-Hours Handler
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Broker doesn't answer.
**Phase**: 6
**Priority**: CRITICAL — 40% of broker calls go to voicemail

---

## Purpose

Convert a missed call into a booked load through systematic multi-channel follow-up. Never let a good load die because a broker didn't pick up on the first try.

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Leave Professional Voicemail (<20 seconds)

Via Bland AI voicemail detection:

```
"Hi, this is [Name] calling from [Carrier Company] — I'm reaching out about 
your [origin] to [destination] load, reference [REF#], for [pickup date]. 
We have equipment available and I'd love to connect. Please call me back 
at [callback number] or I'll try you again shortly. Thanks!"
```

**Voicemail Rules:**
- Under 20 seconds — brokers delete longer ones
- Include: who you are, load reference, callback number
- No rate on voicemail — negotiate live
- Natural, upbeat tone — no urgency/desperation

### Step 2 — Send Follow-Up Email (Within 60 Seconds of Voicemail)

Subject: `[Carrier Company] — Available for Load [REF#] — [Origin] → [Destination]`

Body:
```
Hi [Broker First Name],

Just left you a voicemail about the [origin → destination] load [REF#] for [date].

We have a [equipment type] available in [origin city] and are interested in 
covering this. We're looking for approximately $[market_rate] for this lane — 
happy to discuss.

Feel free to call me at [phone] or reply here. We're ready to move quickly.

[Dispatcher Name]
[Carrier Company] | MC# [XX] | [Phone]
```

### Step 3 — Attempt Schedule

```python
RETRY_SCHEDULE = {
    1: {"delay_minutes": 0,   "action": "voicemail + email"},
    2: {"delay_minutes": 20,  "action": "call only (no voicemail)"},
    3: {"delay_minutes": 60,  "action": "email only (shorter, different subject)"},
}

def schedule_retry(broker_id: str, load_id: str, attempt: int):
    if attempt > 3:
        # Exhausted — mark broker as unreachable for this load
        tms.update_load(load_id, broker_status="EXHAUSTED")
        # Move to next load candidate
        return "MOVE_TO_NEXT_LOAD"
    
    delay = RETRY_SCHEDULE[attempt]["delay_minutes"]
    next_attempt_time = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=delay)
    
    queue.schedule("broker_call_retry", {
        "broker_id": broker_id,
        "load_id": load_id,
        "attempt": attempt,
    }, run_at=next_attempt_time)
    
    return next_attempt_time
```

### Step 4 — After-Hours Detection

```python
def is_after_hours(broker_timezone: str = "America/Chicago") -> bool:
    broker_time = datetime.now(pytz.timezone(broker_timezone))
    hour = broker_time.hour
    weekday = broker_time.weekday()  # 0=Mon, 6=Sun
    
    # After hours: before 7 AM, after 6 PM, or weekend
    if weekday >= 5:  # Weekend
        return True
    if hour < 7 or hour >= 18:
        return True
    return False

# If after hours: don't leave voicemail — schedule first call for 7 AM
# Some brokers DO answer after hours — still try, just don't repeat
```

### Step 5 — Meanwhile, Keep Searching

While retries are scheduled:
1. Continue load board search for this carrier
2. If another eligible load is found → work that in parallel
3. If carrier confirms another load → cancel remaining retries on original
4. If original load books via email reply → cancel competing load search

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Voicemail full | Note in broker CRM; send email only |
| Broker calls back after hours | Route to human escalation if outside bot hours |
| Email bounces | Try alternative broker email from CRM |
| Load still posted after 3 attempts | Flag for human call |

# SKILL: Multilingual Communications Engine
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Any communication to a carrier — auto-translates if needed.
**Phase**: All
**Priority**: HIGH

---

## Purpose

A significant portion of owner-operators primarily communicate in Spanish. Missing a YES/NO confirmation because of a language barrier costs a load booking. This skill ensures every carrier communicates in their strongest language.

---

## Supported Languages

| Language | Code | Carrier Base % | Priority |
|----------|------|---------------|---------|
| English | en | ~65% | Full support |
| Spanish | es | ~30% | Full support |
| Portuguese (Brazilian) | pt-BR | ~3% | Full support |
| Haitian Creole | ht | ~1% | Basic support |
| Other | — | ~1% | English fallback + flag |

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Language Detection

```python
def detect_carrier_language(carrier_id: str, inbound_message: str = None) -> str:
    # Priority 1: Stored preference in carrier profile
    carrier = db.get_carrier(carrier_id)
    if carrier.language_preference:
        return carrier.language_preference
    
    # Priority 2: Detect from incoming message
    if inbound_message:
        detected = langdetect.detect(inbound_message)
        if detected in SUPPORTED_LANGUAGES:
            # Save preference for future
            db.update_carrier(carrier_id, language_preference=detected)
            return detected
    
    # Default: English
    return "en"
```

### Step 2 — Translation with Trucking Context

```python
async def translate_dispatch_message(content: str, target_lang: str) -> str:
    if target_lang == "en":
        return content  # No translation needed
    
    response = await openai.chat.completions.create(
        model="gpt-4o-mini",
        messages=[
            {
                "role": "system",
                "content": f"""You are a professional truck dispatch translator.
                Translate to {target_lang}. Preserve all:
                - Numbers (rates, weights, times, distances)
                - Load reference numbers exactly
                - Addresses exactly (do not translate city/street names)
                - Industry terms (BOL, RC, TONU, detention, lumper — keep in English or use standard industry Spanish)
                - Urgency level of the original
                Translate naturally and professionally.""",
            },
            {"role": "user", "content": content},
        ],
        max_tokens=500,
    )
    
    return response.choices[0].message.content

# Example:
# English: "LOAD OFFER — Reply YES or NO: PU: Nashville, TN | Rate: $2.82/mile"
# Spanish: "OFERTA DE CARGA — Responda SÍ o NO: Recogida: Nashville, TN | Tarifa: $2.82/milla"
```

### Step 3 — Inbound Response Processing

When carrier replies in Spanish:

```python
async def process_multilingual_response(message: str, carrier_id: str) -> dict:
    language = detect_carrier_language(carrier_id, message)
    
    if language != "en":
        # Translate to English for processing
        english_version = await translate_to_english(message)
    else:
        english_version = message
    
    # Process English version through normal response detection
    intent = detect_response_intent(english_version)
    
    return {
        "original": message,
        "english": english_version,
        "intent": intent,  # CONFIRMED / REJECTED / QUESTION / UNCLEAR
        "language": language,
    }
```

### Step 4 — Common Trucking Phrases Reference (Spanish)

```python
SPANISH_TRUCKING_TERMS = {
    # Confirmations
    "sí|si|confirmo|ok|bueno|dale|voy|acepto": "CONFIRMED",
    "no|no puedo|no me funciona|paso": "REJECTED",
    
    # Status updates
    "cargado|saliendo|en camino": "LOADED_DEPARTING",
    "llegué|llegue|aquí estoy": "ARRIVED",
    "entregado|terminé|listo": "DELIVERED",
    
    # Issues  
    "falla|problema|choque|accidente|desgonflado": "BREAKDOWN",
    "demora|tarde|tráfico": "DELAY",
    "ayuda|emergencia": "EMERGENCY",
}
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Language not in supported list | Send in English, flag carrier profile for review |
| Translation produces gibberish | Fall back to English, log for review |
| Carrier mixes English and Spanish | Detect dominant language; translate only the non-dominant portions |

skill_id: "J-whatsapp-conversation-manager"
name: "WhatsApp Conversation Manager"
version: "1.0.0"

# SKILL: WhatsApp Conversation Manager
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Every inbound WhatsApp message from any driver.
**Phase**: All
**Priority**: HIGH

---

## Purpose

Manage 50+ simultaneous WhatsApp conversations across all active drivers without cross-talk, context loss, or missed messages. Each conversation must maintain context so "YES" from Driver A doesn't get processed as a response from Driver B.

---

## Architecture

### Conversation Context Store (Redis)

```python
# Each driver has their own conversation context
async def get_conversation_context(phone_number: str) -> dict:
    key = f"cortex:wa:context:{phone_number}"
    raw = await redis.get(key)
    
    if raw:
        return json.loads(raw)
    
    # New conversation — look up carrier by phone
    carrier = await db.get_carrier_by_phone(phone_number)
    
    return {
        "phone": phone_number,
        "carrier_id": carrier.id if carrier else None,
        "carrier_name": carrier.name if carrier else "Unknown",
        "language": carrier.language_preference if carrier else "en",
        "current_load_id": carrier.active_load_id if carrier else None,
        "awaiting": None,         # What response is the bot waiting for?
        "conversation_history": [],
        "last_message_at": None,
    }

async def save_conversation_context(phone: str, context: dict):
    key = f"cortex:wa:context:{phone}"
    await redis.setex(key, 86400, json.dumps(context))  # 24-hour TTL
```

### Inbound Message Processing

```python
async def process_inbound_whatsapp(webhook: dict):
    from_number = webhook["From"].replace("whatsapp:", "")
    body = webhook.get("Body", "")
    media_urls = [webhook.get(f"MediaUrl{i}") for i in range(10) if webhook.get(f"MediaUrl{i}")]
    
    # Load conversation context
    context = await get_conversation_context(from_number)
    
    # Translate if needed
    if context["language"] != "en":
        english_body = await multilingual_engine.translate_to_english(body)
    else:
        english_body = body
    
    # Handle media attachments (BOL photos, POD, documents)
    if media_urls:
        await handle_media_attachment(media_urls, context, english_body)
        return
    
    # Determine response based on what bot is awaiting
    if context["awaiting"] == "LOAD_CONFIRMATION":
        await handle_load_confirmation_response(english_body, context)
    elif context["awaiting"] == "CHECK_CALL":
        await handle_check_call_response(english_body, context)
    elif context["awaiting"] == "POD_DOCUMENTS":
        await handle_pod_response(english_body, context)
    else:
        # General message — route through event router
        await event_router.route("WHATSAPP_INBOUND", {
            "body": english_body,
            "carrier_id": context["carrier_id"],
            "context": context,
        })
    
    # Append to conversation history
    context["conversation_history"].append({
        "role": "driver",
        "content": body,
        "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
    })
    context["last_message_at"] = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
    await save_conversation_context(from_number, context)
```

### Outbound Message Sender

```python
async def send_whatsapp(to_phone: str, message: str, media_url: str = None):
    # Translate if carrier's language is not English
    context = await get_conversation_context(to_phone)
    
    if context["language"] != "en":
        translated = await multilingual_engine.translate(message, context["language"])
    else:
        translated = message
    
    # Send via Twilio
    twilio_client.messages.create(
        from_=f"whatsapp:{TWILIO_WHATSAPP_NUMBER}",
        to=f"whatsapp:{to_phone}",
        body=translated,
        media_url=[media_url] if media_url else None,
    )
    
    # Log in conversation history
    context["conversation_history"].append({
        "role": "bot",
        "content": translated,
        "original_english": message,
        "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
    })
    await save_conversation_context(to_phone, context)
```

---

## Cross-Thread Safety

When 50 carriers are active, messages must never mix:

```python
# Each carrier's context is isolated by phone number key in Redis
# No shared state between carrier conversations
# Locks acquired per carrier for any write operation

async def safe_context_update(phone: str, updater_func):
    lock = f"cortex:wa:lock:{phone}"
    async with redis_lock(lock, timeout=5):
        context = await get_conversation_context(phone)
        updated = updater_func(context)
        await save_conversation_context(phone, updated)
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Driver sends message with no active load | Respond with availability prompt |
| Message from unknown number | Respond asking them to identify themselves |
| Twilio delivery failure | Retry 3x; switch to SMS fallback |
| Context cache miss | Rebuild from database |

# SKILL: Call Recording & Transcription
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Every completed broker call.
**Phase**: 6–7
**Priority**: HIGH

---

## Purpose

Transcribe every broker call for three critical reasons: (1) extract structured data when AI voice doesn't capture it cleanly, (2) provide irrefutable evidence in rate/detention/claim disputes, (3) create training data for negotiation improvement.

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Download and Store Recording

```python
async def process_call_recording(call_id: str, recording_url: str, metadata: dict):
    # Download recording from Bland AI
    audio_data = await http.get(recording_url)
    
    # Store in S3 with standardized path
    s3_key = f"recordings/{metadata['carrier_id']}/{metadata['load_id']}/{call_id}.mp3"
    await s3.upload(s3_key, audio_data, {
        "ContentType": "audio/mpeg",
        "Metadata": {
            "call_id": call_id,
            "load_id": metadata.get("load_id", ""),
            "duration": str(metadata.get("duration", 0)),
            "broker_phone": metadata.get("broker_phone", ""),
        }
    })
    
    return f"s3://cortex-recordings/{s3_key}"
```

### Step 2 — Transcription via Deepgram

```python
async def transcribe_call(recording_s3_url: str) -> dict:
    deepgram = Deepgram(DEEPGRAM_API_KEY)
    
    response = await deepgram.transcription.pre_recorded({
        "url": recording_s3_url,
    }, {
        "punctuate": True,
        "diarize": True,      # Speaker identification
        "smart_format": True,
        "model": "nova-2",
        "language": "en-US",
        "keywords": [         # Boost accuracy for freight terms
            "detention:2",
            "TONU:3",
            "lumper:2",
            "BOL:3",
            "factoring:2",
            "accessorial:2",
            "rate confirmation:2",
        ],
    })
    
    transcript = response["results"]["channels"][0]["alternatives"][0]["transcript"]
    
    # Format with speaker labels
    paragraphs = response["results"]["channels"][0]["alternatives"][0].get("paragraphs", {})
    formatted = format_with_speakers(paragraphs)
    
    return {
        "raw_transcript": transcript,
        "formatted_transcript": formatted,
        "confidence": response["results"]["channels"][0]["alternatives"][0]["confidence"],
        "duration_seconds": response["metadata"]["duration"],
    }
```

### Step 3 — Structured Data Extraction

```python
async def extract_call_data(transcript: str, metadata: dict) -> dict:
    response = await openai.chat.completions.create(
        model="claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
        messages=[
            {
                "role": "system",
                "content": """Extract structured data from this freight broker call transcript.
                Return JSON with these fields (null if not mentioned):
                {
                  "outcome": "BOOKED | RATE_TOO_LOW | NO_ANSWER | LOAD_COVERED | CARRIER_REJECTED",
                  "agreed_rate_per_mile": float or null,
                  "agreed_flat_rate": float or null,
                  "detention_free_hours": int or null,
                  "detention_rate_per_hour": float or null,
                  "tonu_amount": float or null,
                  "lumper_payer": "broker | carrier | null",
                  "pickup_address": string or null,
                  "delivery_address": string or null,
                  "pickup_datetime": string or null,
                  "delivery_datetime": string or null,
                  "commodity": string or null,
                  "weight_lbs": int or null,
                  "payment_terms": string or null,
                  "tracking_requirement": string or null,
                  "broker_contact_name": string or null,
                  "mc_number_provided": string or null,
                  "carrier_email_provided": string or null
                }"""
            },
            {"role": "user", "content": transcript}
        ],
        max_tokens=500,
        response_format={"type": "json_object"},
    )
    
    return json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Step 4 — Index for Dispute Search

```python
async def index_transcript(transcript_data: dict, metadata: dict):
    await elasticsearch.index(
        index="call_transcripts",
        document={
            "call_id": metadata["call_id"],
            "load_id": metadata.get("load_id"),
            "carrier_id": metadata.get("carrier_id"),
            "broker_name": metadata.get("broker_name"),
            "transcript": transcript_data["raw_transcript"],
            "structured_data": transcript_data.get("structured_data"),
            "call_date": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "recording_url": metadata["recording_s3_url"],
        }
    )
    # Now searchable: "Find all calls where detention was discussed with Echo Global"
```

---

## Dispute Evidence Protocol

When a broker disputes a rate or accessorial:

```python
async def pull_dispute_evidence(load_id: str, dispute_type: str) -> dict:
    # Search transcript for relevant mentions
    results = await elasticsearch.search(
        index="call_transcripts",
        query={
            "bool": {
                "must": [
                    {"term": {"load_id": load_id}},
                    {"match": {"transcript": dispute_type}},
                ]
            }
        }
    )
    
    if results["hits"]["total"]["value"] > 0:
        transcript = results["hits"]["hits"][0]["_source"]
        return {
            "evidence_found": True,
            "recording_url": transcript["recording_url"],
            "relevant_quote": extract_relevant_quote(transcript["transcript"], dispute_type),
            "call_date": transcript["call_date"],
        }
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Deepgram API unavailable | Use OpenAI Whisper as fallback |
| Low confidence transcript (<0.7) | Flag for human review; still store |
| Call too short (<30s) | Likely voicemail or hung up; log minimal data |
| Recording download fails | Retry 3x; log missing recording in TMS |

# SKILL: API Integration Gateway
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Any skill needing external API access.
**Phase**: All
**Priority**: CRITICAL

---

## Purpose

Centralize all external API calls through one gateway that handles authentication, rate limiting, caching, retries, and circuit breaking. No skill should ever make a raw HTTP request — everything goes through this gateway.

---

## Integration Catalog

```python
API_CONFIGS = {
    "dat_load_board": {
        "base_url": "https://api.dat.com/",
        "auth_type": "oauth2",
        "rate_limit": {"requests_per_minute": 60},
        "cache_ttl": {"search_results": 180, "rate_data": 900},  # seconds
        "retry": {"max_attempts": 3, "backoff": "exponential"},
```

### Request Execution

```python
class APIGateway:
    def __init__(self):
        self.circuit_breakers = {}
        self.cache = RedisCache()
        self.secrets = AWSSecretsManager()
    
    async def call(self, api_name: str, endpoint: str, method: str = "GET",
                   payload: dict = None, cache_key: str = None) -> dict:
        
        config = API_CONFIGS[api_name]
        
        # Check circuit breaker
        if self.is_circuit_open(api_name):
            return await self.use_fallback(api_name, endpoint, payload)
        
        # Check cache
        if cache_key and method == "GET":
            cached = await self.cache.get(f"{api_name}:{cache_key}")
            if cached:
                return {"data": cached, "from_cache": True}
        
        # Get auth credentials
        auth = await self.get_auth(api_name, config["auth_type"])
        
        # Execute with retry
        for attempt in range(config["retry"]["max_attempts"]):
            try:
                start_time = time.time()
                response = await self.http_client.request(
                    method=method,
                    url=f"{config['base_url']}{endpoint}",
                    headers=auth["headers"],
                    json=payload,
                    timeout=30,
                )
                latency_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                
                # Record success
                self.record_success(api_name, latency_ms)
                
                # Cache if appropriate
                if cache_key and method == "GET":
                    ttl = config.get("cache_ttl", {}).get(cache_key, 300)
                    await self.cache.set(f"{api_name}:{cache_key}", response.json(), ttl)
                
                # Log to Datadog
                datadog.histogram(f"api.latency.{api_name}", latency_ms)
                
                return {"data": response.json(), "latency_ms": latency_ms, "from_cache": False}
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.record_failure(api_name)
                
                if attempt < config["retry"]["max_attempts"] - 1:
                    wait = self.calculate_backoff(config["retry"]["backoff"], attempt)
                    await asyncio.sleep(wait)
                else:
                    # All retries exhausted
                    if "fallback" in config:
                        return await self.use_fallback(api_name, endpoint, payload)
                    raise APIGatewayError(f"{api_name} failed after {attempt+1} attempts: {e}")
    
    async def get_auth(self, api_name: str, auth_type: str) -> dict:
        secret = await self.secrets.get_secret(f"cortex/{api_name}")
        
        if auth_type == "api_key":
            return {"headers": {"X-API-Key": secret["api_key"]}}
        elif auth_type == "bearer":
            return {"headers": {"Authorization": f"Bearer {secret['token']}"}}
        elif auth_type == "oauth2":
            token = await self.get_or_refresh_oauth_token(api_name, secret)
            return {"headers": {"Authorization": f"Bearer {token}"}}
        elif auth_type == "basic":
            encoded = base64.b64encode(f"{secret['username']}:{secret['password']}".encode()).decode()
            return {"headers": {"Authorization": f"Basic {encoded}"}}
```

---

## Circuit Breaker

```python
def is_circuit_open(self, api_name: str) -> bool:
    cb = self.circuit_breakers.get(api_name, {"failures": 0, "last_failure": None, "state": "CLOSED"})
    
    config = API_CONFIGS[api_name].get("circuit_breaker", {})
    threshold = config.get("failure_threshold", 5)
    recovery_timeout = config.get("recovery_timeout", 60)
    
    if cb["state"] == "OPEN":
        if (datetime.utcnow() - cb["last_failure"]).seconds > recovery_timeout:
            cb["state"] = "HALF-OPEN"  # Allow one test request
            return False
        return True  # Still open
    
    return False

def record_failure(self, api_name: str):
    cb = self.circuit_breakers.setdefault(api_name, {"failures": 0, "state": "CLOSED"})
    cb["failures"] += 1
    cb["last_failure"] = datetime.utcnow()
    
    threshold = API_CONFIGS[api_name].get("circuit_breaker", {}).get("failure_threshold", 5)
    if cb["failures"] >= threshold:
        cb["state"] = "OPEN"
        alert(f"Circuit breaker OPEN for {api_name}")
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| OAuth token expired | Auto-refresh; retry original request |
| Rate limit hit | Back off for window duration; queue request |
| API returns 5xx | Retry with exponential backoff |
| API returns 4xx | Log error; do not retry; return structured error |
| All fallbacks exhausted | Human escalation with context |

# SKILL: Document OCR Intelligence
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Any document received from any source.
**Phase**: All
**Priority**: CRITICAL

---

## Purpose

Read every piece of freight paperwork automatically — rate confirmations, bills of lading, certificates of insurance, W-9s, lumper receipts — and extract structured data without human involvement. Referenced by 8 other skills but formally defined here.

---

## Document Type Handlers

### Rate Confirmation (RC)

```python
RC_FIELDS = {
    "carrier_mc_number":      r"MC[\s#-]*(\d{5,8})",
    "broker_mc_number":       r"Broker.*MC[\s#-]*(\d{5,8})",
    "load_reference":         r"(Load\s*#?|Ref\s*#?|Order\s*#?)\s*([A-Z0-9\-]+)",
    "pickup_address":         "extract from SHIPPER section",
    "pickup_date":            "extract from PICKUP DATE section",
    "pickup_appointment":     "extract from APPOINTMENT or WINDOW",
    "delivery_address":       "extract from CONSIGNEE section",
    "delivery_date":          "extract from DELIVERY DATE section",
    "commodity":              "extract from COMMODITY or FREIGHT",
    "weight":                 r"(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*)\s*(?:lbs?|pounds?)",
    "rate_per_mile":          r"\$\s*(\d+\.\d{2})\s*(?:per\s*mile|\/mile|cpm)",
    "flat_rate":              r"(?:flat|total|all-in).*\$\s*(\d+(?:\.\d{2})?)",
    "detention_rate":         r"detention.*\$\s*(\d+(?:\.\d{2})?)\s*(?:per\s*hour|\/hr)",
    "detention_free_hours":   r"(\d+)\s*(?:free\s*hours?|hrs?\s*free)",
    "tonu_amount":            r"(?:tonu|truck order not used).*\$\s*(\d+(?:\.\d{2})?)",
    "payment_terms":          r"Net\s*(\d+)",
    "factoring_notice":       "contains NOA | factoring | remit to",
}
```

### Bill of Lading (BOL)

```python
BOL_FIELDS = {
    "shipper_name":           "SHIPPER section",
    "consignee_name":         "CONSIGNEE section", 
    "pickup_address":         "FROM address",
    "delivery_address":       "TO address",
    "commodity_description":  "COMMODITY / DESCRIPTION OF ARTICLES",
    "piece_count":            r"(\d+)\s*(?:pallets?|pieces?|cases?|drums?|units?)",
    "total_weight":           r"(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})*)\s*(?:lbs?|pounds?)",
    "pickup_time_in":         "time in / arrival time at pickup",
    "pickup_time_out":        "time out / departure time from pickup",
    "delivery_time_in":       "time in / arrival time at delivery",
    "delivery_time_out":      "time out / departure from delivery",
    "receiver_signature":     "presence and legibility of delivery signature",
    "exceptions_noted":       "any damage notations or exceptions on BOL",
}
```
