```python
    "business_name":          "Line 2 — Business name if different",
    "tax_classification":     "checkbox: Individual/Sole prop | LLC | C Corp | S Corp | Partnership",
    "ein":                    r"Employer ID.*(\d{2}-\d{7})",
    "ssn":                    r"Social Security.*(\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4})",  # Masked in storage
    "address":                "Lines 5-6",
    "signature_present":      "boolean — is signature present",
    "date_signed":            "date field",
}
```

---

## Extraction Pipeline

```python
async def extract_document(doc_url: str, doc_type: str, context: dict) -> dict:
    
    # Step 1: Download document
    doc_bytes = await download_document(doc_url)
    
    # Step 2: Detect document type if UNKNOWN
    if doc_type == "UNKNOWN":
        doc_type = await detect_document_type(doc_bytes)
    
    # Step 3: Primary OCR — AWS Textract
    try:
        textract_result = await textract_extract(doc_bytes, doc_type)
        raw_text = textract_result["text"]
        tables = textract_result["tables"]
        forms = textract_result["key_value_pairs"]
        confidence = textract_result["avg_confidence"]
    except Exception:
        # Fallback to Google Document AI
        raw_text, tables, forms, confidence = await google_doc_ai_extract(doc_bytes)
    
    # Step 4: Claude Vision for contextual understanding
    if confidence < 0.85 or doc_type in ["BOL", "LUMPER_RECEIPT"]:
        # Use Claude Vision for complex layouts and handwritten content
        vision_result = await claude_vision_extract(doc_bytes, doc_type)
        # Merge: prefer Claude Vision for low-confidence Textract fields
        fields = merge_extraction_results(textract_result, vision_result)
    else:
        fields = extract_fields_by_type(raw_text, forms, tables, doc_type)
    
    # Step 5: Validate extracted fields
    validation_issues = validate_fields(fields, doc_type)
    
    # Step 6: Store document
    s3_path = await store_document(doc_bytes, doc_type, context)
    
    # Step 7: Return structured result
    return {
        "document_type": doc_type,
        "fields": fields,
        "validation_issues": validation_issues,
        "confidence": confidence,
        "s3_path": s3_path,
        "raw_text": raw_text,
    }

async def claude_vision_extract(doc_bytes: bytes, doc_type: str) -> dict:
    base64_image = base64.b64encode(doc_bytes).decode()
    
    field_list = list(DOCUMENT_FIELDS[doc_type].keys())
    
    response = await anthropic.messages.create(
        model="claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
        max_tokens=1000,
        messages=[
            {
                "role": "user",
                "content": [
                    {
                        "type": "image",
                        "source": {
                            "type": "base64",
                            "media_type": "image/jpeg",
                            "data": base64_image,
                        },
                    },
                    {
                        "type": "text",
                        "text": f"""Extract these fields from this {doc_type} document:
                        {json.dumps(field_list)}
                        
                        Return as JSON. Use null for missing fields.
                        For times: use HH:MM format.
                        For dates: use YYYY-MM-DD format.
                        For money: return as float without $ signs.""",
                    },
                ],
            }
        ],
    )
    
    return json.loads(response.content[0].text)
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Document unreadable (blurry/dark) | Request retake from driver; flag quality issue |
| Critical field missing | Return partial data with missing_fields list |
| Textract and Claude Vision disagree | Flag for human review on conflicting field |
| Document appears fraudulent | Flag immediately; route to fraud detection |
| PDF password-protected | Alert sender to provide unlocked version |

# SKILL: Email Parsing Automation
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Every inbound email to dispatch inbox.
**Phase**: All
**Priority**: CRITICAL — without this, a human reads every email

---

## Purpose

Process every incoming email automatically — classify what it is, extract relevant data, route to the right skill, and optionally send an auto-reply. Zero emails require human reading unless explicitly escalated.

---

## Email Classification

```python
async def classify_email(email: dict) -> str:
    subject = email["subject"].lower()
    body = email["body"].lower()
    sender = email["from"].lower()
    has_pdf = any(att["content_type"] == "application/pdf" for att in email["attachments"])
    
    # Rule-based fast path
    rules = [
        # Rate Confirmation
        (lambda: any(kw in subject for kw in ["rate confirmation", "rate con", "rc#", "load confirmation"]) or
                 (has_pdf and any(kw in body for kw in ["rate per mile", "pickup address", "delivery address"])),
         "RC"),
        
        # Carrier Packet / Setup
        (lambda: any(kw in subject for kw in ["carrier packet", "carrier setup", "setup packet", "new carrier"]),
         "CARRIER_PACKET"),
        
        # Payment / Remittance
        (lambda: any(kw in subject for kw in ["payment", "remittance", "ach", "check", "wire", "paid"]) or
                 any(kw in body for kw in ["payment enclosed", "please find payment", "ach initiated"]),
         "PAYMENT"),
        
        # Detention / Dispute
        (lambda: any(kw in subject for kw in ["detention", "accessorial", "dispute", "claim", "short pay"]),
         "DETENTION_DISPUTE"),
        
        # Compliance
        (lambda: any(kw in subject for kw in ["insurance", "coi", "certificate", "fmcsa", "compliance"]),
         "COMPLIANCE"),
        
        # Load Tender (EDI)
        (lambda: any(kw in subject for kw in ["load tender", "tender", "edi 204"]) or
                 sender.endswith((".shipper.com", ".walmart.com", ".amazon.com")),
         "LOAD_TENDER"),
    ]
    
    for condition, category in rules:
        if condition():
            return category
    
    # LLM classification for ambiguous emails
    return await llm_classify_email(email["subject"], email["body"][:500])

async def llm_classify_email(subject: str, body: str) -> str:
    response = await openai.chat.completions.create(
        model="gpt-4o-mini",
        messages=[
            {
                "role": "system",
                "content": """Classify this trucking dispatch email into exactly ONE category:
                RC, CARRIER_PACKET, PAYMENT, DETENTION_DISPUTE, COMPLIANCE,
                LOAD_TENDER, BROKER_COMMUNICATION, CARRIER_COMMUNICATION, 
                INVOICE_REQUEST, OTHER.
                Reply with ONLY the category name.""",
            },
            {"role": "user", "content": f"Subject: {subject}\n\nBody: {body}"},
        ],
        max_tokens=20,
    )
    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()
```

### Processing Per Category

```python
EMAIL_HANDLERS = {
    "RC": handle_rate_confirmation_email,        # → skill 12 (rate-confirmation-review)
    "CARRIER_PACKET": handle_carrier_packet,     # → skill 11 (carrier-packet-completion)
    "PAYMENT": handle_payment_email,             # → skill 19 (payment-reconciliation)
    "DETENTION_DISPUTE": handle_dispute_email,   # → human escalation
    "COMPLIANCE": handle_compliance_email,       # → skill 26 (compliance-monitoring)
    "LOAD_TENDER": handle_load_tender,           # → skill O (EDI integration)
    "OTHER": handle_generic_email,               # → TMS log + human review queue
}

async def handle_rate_confirmation_email(email: dict):
    # Extract PDF attachment
    pdf_attachment = next(
        (att for att in email["attachments"] if att["content_type"] == "application/pdf"),
        None
    )
    
    if pdf_attachment:
        # Run OCR to extract all RC fields
        extracted = await document_ocr.extract(
            pdf_attachment["url"],
            doc_type="RC",
            context={"sender": email["from"]},
        )
        
        # Find the matching load in TMS by broker email + reference
        load = await tms.find_load_by_broker_email(email["from"])
        
        if load:
            # Trigger rate confirmation review
            await rate_confirmation_review.start(
                load_id=load.id,
                rc_data=extracted["fields"],
                rc_pdf_url=extracted["s3_path"],
            )
        else:
            # RC for a load we don't have yet — escalate
            await human_escalation.create(
                reason="RC_WITHOUT_MATCHING_LOAD",
                context={"email": email, "extracted": extracted},
            )
    
    # Auto-reply acknowledgement
    await send_email_reply(email, "RC received — reviewing now.")
```

================================================================================
# SKILL P — Data Backup & Recovery
================================================================================

---
skill_id: "P-data-backup-recovery"
name: "Data Backup & Recovery"
version: "1.0.0"
phase: 0
priority: medium
trigger: "Continuous automated backups. Also triggered on system health alerts or manual DR invocation."
inputs:
  - backup_scope: "enum: FULL | INCREMENTAL | SNAPSHOT"
  - recovery_target: "optional — load_id, carrier_id, or full system"
outputs:
  - backup_manifest: "list of all backup artifacts with checksums"
  - recovery_report: "what was restored and from which checkpoint"
  - rpo_rto_status: "current recovery point and time objectives"
integrations:
  - AWS RDS (PostgreSQL automated backups)
  - AWS S3 (document vault)
  - AWS ElastiCache Redis (state snapshots)
  - LangGraph checkpoint store (PostgreSQL)
  - PagerDuty (DR alerts)
depends_on: []
triggers_next: []
tags: [backup, recovery, disaster-recovery, rpo, rto, business-continuity]
---

## Purpose

Ensure that a complete system failure, database corruption, or mid-load crash never permanently loses carrier data, load records, or financial history. Maintain defined RPO (Recovery Point Objective) and RTO (Recovery Time Objective) targets.

## SLA Targets

| Objective | Target | Notes |
|-----------|--------|-------|
| RPO (max data loss) | 15 minutes | Continuous WAL archiving on RDS |
| RTO (max downtime) | 30 minutes | ECS blue/green deployment |
| Document vault | 99.999% durability | AWS S3 with versioning + replication |
| LangGraph checkpoints | Never lost | Written to PostgreSQL before each node |
| Redis state | Best-effort | Rebuilt from PostgreSQL on restart |

## Backup Architecture

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  PostgreSQL (RDS Multi-AZ)                      │
│  ├─ Continuous WAL archiving → S3               │
│  ├─ Automated daily snapshots (7-day PITR)      │
│  └─ Cross-region replica → us-west-2            │
│                                                 │
│  AWS S3 (Documents)                             │
│  ├─ Versioning enabled on all buckets           │
│  ├─ Cross-region replication → us-west-2        │
│  └─ Lifecycle: 30d → IA, 1yr → Glacier         │
│                                                 │
│  Redis (ElastiCache)                            │
│  ├─ AOF persistence enabled (every second)      │
│  └─ Redis snapshot every 15 minutes             │
│                                                 │
│  LangGraph Checkpoints                          │
│  └─ Written to PostgreSQL (cortex_checkpoints)  │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Continuous Database Backup (Always Running)

  backup_retention_period    = 7      # 7-day PITR

# SKILL: Dispatcher Fee Collection
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Load paid by broker → calculate and collect dispatch fee.
**Phase**: 17
**Priority**: CRITICAL — this is the revenue engine of the entire business

---

## Purpose

Calculate and collect the dispatch service fee for every load. Without this skill, Cortex Bot provides all its services for free. This is how the business generates revenue.

---

## Fee Structure Models

```python
FEE_MODELS = {
    "percentage": {
        "description": "% of gross load revenue",
        "typical_range": "5–8%",
        "calculation": lambda gross, pct: gross * pct,
        "best_for": "Variable volume carriers, new relationships",
    },
    "flat_weekly": {
        "description": "Fixed fee per truck per week",
        "typical_range": "$300–650/week",
        "calculation": lambda trucks, rate: trucks * rate,
        "billing_cycle": "weekly",
        "best_for": "High-volume carriers with consistent loads",
    },
    "hybrid": {
        "description": "Base weekly + % per load",
        "typical": "$150/week + 3% of gross",
        "calculation": lambda gross, pct, base: base + (gross * pct),
        "best_for": "Established carriers — aligns incentives",
    },
    "per_load_flat": {
        "description": "Fixed $ per load regardless of revenue",
        "typical_range": "$50–150/load",
        "calculation": lambda loads, rate: loads * rate,
        "best_for": "Short-haul, high-frequency runs",
    },
}
```

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Calculate Fee When Load Paid

```python
async def calculate_dispatch_fee(load_id: str, gross_revenue: float) -> dict:
    # Get this carrier's fee agreement
    carrier = await db.get_carrier_by_load(load_id)
    agreement = carrier.dispatch_agreement
    
    model = agreement["model"]  # percentage | flat_weekly | hybrid | per_load_flat
    
    if model == "percentage":
        fee_pct = agreement["percentage"]  # e.g., 0.06 = 6%
        fee_amount = gross_revenue * fee_pct
        
    elif model == "flat_weekly":
        # Already collected in weekly cycle — skip per-load collection
        return {"fee_model": "flat_weekly", "collected_in_cycle": True}
    
    elif model == "hybrid":
        base_weekly = agreement["base_weekly"]
        fee_pct = agreement["percentage"]
        fee_amount = (base_weekly / 5) + (gross_revenue * fee_pct)  # Prorate daily
        
    elif model == "per_load_flat":
        fee_amount = agreement["per_load_rate"]
    
    net_carrier = gross_revenue - fee_amount
    
    return {
        "gross_revenue": gross_revenue,
        "fee_model": model,
        "fee_amount": round(fee_amount, 2),
        "fee_percentage": fee_amount / gross_revenue,
        "net_carrier": round(net_carrier, 2),
        "load_id": load_id,
        "carrier_id": carrier.id,
    }
```

### Step 2 — Generate Dispatch Fee Invoice

```
DISPATCH SERVICE FEE INVOICE

From: [Dispatch Service Name]
      [Address]
      [EIN]

To:   [Carrier Company Name]
      MC# [XX] | [Owner Name]

Invoice #: DISP-[LoadRef]-[Date]
Invoice Date: [Today]

LOAD SUMMARY:
Load #: [TMS Load ID]
Route: [Origin] → [Destination]  
Pickup: [Date] | Delivery: [Date]
Gross Freight Revenue: $[X]

DISPATCH SERVICE FEE:
Rate: [X%] of gross freight revenue
Fee: $[X.XX]

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
TOTAL DUE: $[Fee Amount]

Services rendered:
✓ Load board search and triage
✓ Broker negotiation and rate locking
✓ Carrier packet and RC processing
✓ Driver dispatch and in-transit monitoring
✓ Detention tracking and documentation
✓ POD collection and invoice submission
✓ Payment follow-up

Payment due: Upon receipt
Pay via: ACH to [bank details] or deduct from next settlement
```

### Step 3 — Collect Fee

**Option A — Deduct from Settlement:**
Most common — fee is deducted when driver settlement is calculated (Skill R).

**Option B — Direct ACH Collection:**

```python
async def collect_fee_via_ach(carrier_id: str, amount: float, invoice_id: str):
    carrier = await db.get_carrier(carrier_id)
    
    # Charge carrier's bank account via Stripe
    payment = await stripe.payment_intents.create({
        "amount": int(amount * 100),  # cents
        "currency": "usd",
        "customer": carrier.stripe_customer_id,
        "payment_method": carrier.default_payment_method,
        "confirm": True,
        "description": f"Dispatch fee — Invoice {invoice_id}",
        "metadata": {"invoice_id": invoice_id, "carrier_id": carrier_id},
    })
    
    return payment
```

### Step 4 — Weekly Flat-Fee Billing Cycle

```python
async def weekly_fee_billing():
    """Runs every Monday morning for flat-fee carriers"""
    flat_fee_carriers = await db.get_carriers(fee_model="flat_weekly")
    
    for carrier in flat_fee_carriers:
        weekly_fee = carrier.dispatch_agreement["weekly_rate"]
        
        # Generate weekly invoice
        invoice = generate_weekly_fee_invoice(carrier, weekly_fee)
        
        # Attempt collection
        await collect_fee_via_ach(carrier.id, weekly_fee, invoice.id)
        
        # If ACH fails, deduct from pending settlements
        if not payment_successful:
            await flag_for_settlement_deduction(carrier.id, weekly_fee)
```

### Step 5 — Revenue Tracking

```python
async def record_revenue(fee_data: dict):
    await db.insert("dispatch_fees", {
        "load_id": fee_data["load_id"],
        "carrier_id": fee_data["carrier_id"],
        "gross_revenue": fee_data["gross_revenue"],
        "fee_amount": fee_data["fee_amount"],
        "fee_model": fee_data["fee_model"],
        "collected_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "status": "COLLECTED",
    })
    
    # Sync to QuickBooks
    await quickbooks_sync.record_revenue(fee_data)
    
    # Update weekly/monthly revenue dashboard
    await update_revenue_dashboard(fee_data["fee_amount"])
```

# SKILL: Driver Settlement
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Load paid + all deductions calculated.
**Phase**: 17
**Priority**: CRITICAL

---

## Purpose

Calculate exactly what the driver earns per load, deduct all authorized amounts, issue payment, and deliver a clear settlement sheet. Carriers who don't understand their pay leave. Transparent, fast settlement = carrier retention.

---

## Settlement Calculation

```python
async def calculate_settlement(load_id: str) -> dict:
    load = await db.get_load(load_id)
    carrier = await db.get_carrier(load.carrier_id)
    
    gross_revenue = load.amount_received_from_broker  # actual payment received
    
    # Deductions
    dispatch_fee = load.dispatch_fee_amount
    fuel_advances = load.fuel_advances_issued       # Comcheks, fuel card advances
    lumper_advances = load.lumper_advances           # If carrier-paid lumper
    repair_advances = load.repair_advances           # Emergency roadside paid by dispatch
    other_deductions = load.authorized_deductions    # Any other approved deductions
    
    total_deductions = dispatch_fee + fuel_advances + lumper_advances + repair_advances + other_deductions
    
    net_settlement = gross_revenue - total_deductions
    
    return {
        "load_id": load_id,
        "carrier_id": load.carrier_id,
        "gross_revenue": gross_revenue,
        "deductions": {
            "dispatch_fee": dispatch_fee,
            "fuel_advances": fuel_advances,
            "lumper_advances": lumper_advances,
            "repair_advances": repair_advances,
            "other": other_deductions,
            "total": total_deductions,
        },
        "net_settlement": net_settlement,
        "payment_method": carrier.payment_method,
        "bank_last4": carrier.bank_account_last4,
    }
```

### Settlement Sheet

```
SETTLEMENT STATEMENT

[Dispatch Service] → [Carrier Company] | MC# [XX]
Settlement Date: [Date]
Load #: [TMS Load ID]

─────────────────────────────────────────
EARNINGS
Gross Freight Revenue:            $[X]
  (Broker: [Broker Name] | Ref: [XX])

─────────────────────────────────────────
DEDUCTIONS
Dispatch Service Fee (6%):       -$[X]
Fuel Advance (Comchek #[XX]):     -$[X]
Lumper Advance ([Location]):      -$[X]
─────────────────────────────────────────
NET SETTLEMENT:                   $[X]

Payment via ACH to [Bank] ****[XXXX]
Expected deposit: 1–2 business days

Questions? Reply to this message or call [phone].
─────────────────────────────────────────
YTD Gross Revenue (your truck):   $[X]
YTD Dispatch Fees Paid:           $[X]
YTD Net Earnings:                 $[X]
```

### ACH Payment Execution

```python
async def issue_settlement_payment(settlement: dict):
    carrier = await db.get_carrier(settlement["carrier_id"])
    
    if carrier.payment_method == "ach_stripe":
        transfer = await stripe.transfers.create({
            "amount": int(settlement["net_settlement"] * 100),
            "currency": "usd",
            "destination": carrier.stripe_connected_account_id,
            "description": f"Settlement — Load {settlement['load_id']}",
            "metadata": {"load_id": settlement["load_id"]},
        })
        
    elif carrier.payment_method == "ach_dwolla":
        transfer = await dwolla.create_transfer({
            "source": CORTEX_BANK_FUNDING_SOURCE,
            "destination": carrier.dwolla_funding_source,
            "amount": {"currency": "USD", "value": str(settlement["net_settlement"])},
        })
    
    # Log payment
    await db.update_load(settlement["load_id"], {
        "settlement_paid_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "settlement_amount": settlement["net_settlement"],
        "payment_reference": transfer.id,
    })
    
    return transfer
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Net settlement is negative (advances > earnings) | Do not pay; roll deficit to next load |
| ACH fails (wrong bank details) | Alert carrier immediately; request updated bank info |
| Carrier disputes deduction | Pull advance record and authorization; review with carrier |
| Load not yet paid by broker | Hold settlement until broker pays |

# SKILL: Driver Advance & Comchek Issuance
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Driver requests fuel money, lumper payment, or emergency cash.
**Phase**: 13 (In-Transit)
**Priority**: CRITICAL — drivers call at 2 AM needing money; delays mean stalled loads

---

## Purpose

Issue fuel card codes and cash advances to drivers instantly, 24/7, without requiring a human dispatcher to wake up. Deduct from their next settlement automatically.

---

## Advance Types & Approval Rules

| Type | Max Amount | Pre-Approval | Notes |
|------|-----------|-------------|-------|
| Fuel advance | $400/tank | Auto-approved | Route to cheapest truck stop |
| Lumper payment | Actual cost (up to $300) | Auto-approved with receipt | Must have lumper receipt |
| Emergency repair | Up to $500 | Auto-approved | Require mechanic invoice |
| Emergency cash | Up to $200 | Auto-approved | Limit 1 per load |
| Large advance | >$500 | Requires human approval | Escalate to operator |

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Verify Request

```python
async def validate_advance_request(request: dict) -> dict:
    carrier = await db.get_carrier(request["carrier_id"])
    load = await db.get_load(request["load_id"])
    
    # Must have active load
    if load.status not in ["DISPATCHED", "IN_TRANSIT", "AT_PICKUP", "AT_DELIVERY"]:
        return {"approved": False, "reason": "No active load — advance not available"}
    
    # Check outstanding advance balance
    outstanding = await db.sum_advances(request["carrier_id"], status="UNPAID")
    
    if outstanding > 800:
        return {"approved": False, "reason": "Outstanding advance balance too high. Settle previous advances first."}
    
    # Check amount limits
    max_amount = ADVANCE_LIMITS[request["advance_type"]]
    if request["amount_requested"] > max_amount:
        return {
            "approved": "PARTIAL",
            "approved_amount": max_amount,
            "reason": f"Maximum {request['advance_type']} advance is ${max_amount}",
        }
    
    return {"approved": True, "approved_amount": request["amount_requested"]}
```

### Step 2 — Issue EFS/Comdata Code

```python
async def issue_comdata_code(carrier_id: str, amount: float, advance_type: str) -> dict:
    # Preferred: EFS (broader network acceptance)
    try:
        response = await efs_api.issue_code({
            "amount": amount,
            "type": "FUEL" if advance_type == "FUEL" else "CASH",
            "carrier_reference": carrier_id,
            "expiry_hours": 24,
            "restrictions": {
                "fuel_only": advance_type == "FUEL",
                "valid_locations": "all_efs_network",
            },
        })
        
        return {
            "code": response["check_code"],
            "network": "EFS",
            "amount": amount,
            "expiry": response["expiry_datetime"],
            "valid_at": "Pilot Flying J, Love's, TA, Petro, and 15,000+ locations",
        }
    
    except EFSAPIError:
        # Fallback to Comdata
        response = await comdata_api.issue_check_code({
            "amount": amount,
            "card_type": "TCHECK",
        })
        
        return {
            "code": response["check_code"],
            "network": "Comdata",
            "amount": amount,
        }
```

### Step 3 — Deliver to Driver via WhatsApp

```
💳 ADVANCE APPROVED

Type: [Fuel/Lumper/Emergency]
Amount: $[X]
Code: [XXXX-XXXX-XXXX]
Network: [EFS/Comdata]
Valid: 24 hours
Valid at: [network description]

How to use:
→ At fuel desk: Say "EFS check" and give them the code
→ At ATM (cash): Use code at Comdata-compatible ATM

This $[X] will be deducted from your settlement for load [#].

Drive safe 🙏
```

### Step 4 — Log Advance in TMS

```python
await db.insert("driver_advances", {
    "advance_id": generate_id(),
    "carrier_id": carrier_id,
    "load_id": load_id,
    "advance_type": advance_type,
    "amount": amount,
    "check_code": code["code"],
    "network": code["network"],
    "issued_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
    "status": "ISSUED",
    "redeemed": False,
    "settlement_deducted": False,
})
```

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| EFS and Comdata both unavailable | Issue Stripe virtual card as emergency fallback |
| Driver can't find accepting location | Text 3 nearest Pilot/TA/Love's with addresses |
| Advance limit exceeded | Escalate to human; explain max limit to driver |
| Code expires unused | Cancel in system; refund to account |

## Chart of Accounts Mapping

```python
QB_ACCOUNTS = {
    # Income
    "dispatch_fees":          "4000 — Dispatch Service Revenue",
    "setup_fees":             "4010 — Carrier Setup Fees",
    
    # Cost of Revenue
    "llm_api_costs":          "5000 — LLM API Costs",
    "voice_call_costs":       "5010 — Bland AI Voice Costs",
    "eld_api_costs":          "5020 — ELD Integration Costs",
    "sms_whatsapp_costs":     "5030 — Twilio Messaging Costs",
    
    # Operating Expenses
    "aws_infrastructure":     "6000 — Cloud Infrastructure",
    "software_subscriptions": "6010 — SaaS Subscriptions",
    "contractor_payments":    "6020 — Contractor Labor",
    "operator_salaries":      "6030 — Staff Salaries",
    
    # Pass-Through (not revenue)
    "fuel_advances":          "2100 — Driver Advances Payable",
    "lumper_advances":        "2110 — Lumper Advances Payable",
    "carrier_settlements":    "2000 — Carrier Settlements Payable",
}
```

### Sync Logic

```python
async def sync_to_quickbooks(event: dict):
    qb_client = await get_qb_client()
    
    if event["type"] == "DISPATCH_FEE_COLLECTED":
        # Record revenue
        invoice = await qb_client.Invoice.create({
            "CustomerRef": {"value": event["carrier_qb_id"]},
            "Line": [{
                "Amount": event["fee_amount"],
                "DetailType": "SalesItemLineDetail",
                "SalesItemLineDetail": {
                    "ItemRef": {"value": QB_ITEMS["dispatch_fee"]},
                    "Description": f"Dispatch fee — Load {event['load_id']}",
                },
            }],
            "DocNumber": event["invoice_id"],
            "DueDate": event["due_date"],
        })
        
        # If already collected, also record payment
        if event.get("payment_received"):
            await qb_client.Payment.create({
                "CustomerRef": {"value": event["carrier_qb_id"]},
                "TotalAmt": event["fee_amount"],
                "Line": [{"Amount": event["fee_amount"], "LinkedTxn": [{"TxnId": invoice["Id"]}]}],
            })
    
    elif event["type"] == "EXPENSE_RECORDED":
        await qb_client.Bill.create({
            "VendorRef": {"value": get_or_create_vendor(event["vendor"])},
            "Line": [{
                "Amount": event["amount"],
                "DetailType": "AccountBasedExpenseLineDetail",
                "AccountBasedExpenseLineDetail": {
                    "AccountRef": {"value": QB_ACCOUNTS[event["expense_category"]]},
                    "Description": event["description"],
                },
            }],
        })
```

---

## Monthly Reconciliation

```python
async def monthly_reconciliation():
    """First of each month — reconcile TMS records with QuickBooks"""
    
    # Pull all transactions from TMS for last month
    tms_transactions = await db.get_monthly_transactions()
    
    # Pull all transactions from QuickBooks for last month
    qb_transactions = await qb_client.query(
        f"SELECT * FROM Invoice WHERE TxnDate >= '{last_month_start}'"
    )
    
    # Find discrepancies
    tms_total = sum(t["amount"] for t in tms_transactions)
    qb_total = sum(t["Amount"] for t in qb_transactions)
    
    if abs(tms_total - qb_total) > 1.00:  # Allow $1 rounding tolerance
        await human_escalation.create(
            reason="ACCOUNTING_DISCREPANCY",
            context={"tms_total": tms_total, "qb_total": qb_total, "difference": tms_total - qb_total},
        )
```

# SKILL: Expense Tracking Per Load
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Any expense incurred during load execution.
**Phase**: 13 (ongoing)
**Priority**: HIGH

---

## Purpose

Track every cost associated with each load to know the TRUE net profit — not just gross revenue. Without this, you might celebrate a $700 load that cost $650 to execute.

---

## Expense Categories

| Category | Source | Impact |
|----------|--------|--------|
| Fuel | Fuel card data + receipts | Carrier expense (reduces margin) |
| Tolls | EZPass/manual | Carrier expense |
| Scale tickets | Weigh station | Carrier expense |
| Permits | Oversize/overweight | Carrier expense |
| Lumper (carrier-paid) | Receipt photo | Invoiced back to broker |
| Advance repayment | Skills S settlement | Deducted from settlement |
| Repair/breakdown | Invoice | Emergency advance |
| Parking | Receipt | Carrier expense |

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Automated Expense Capture

```python
# Fuel card integration — auto-capture fuel purchases
async def sync_fuel_card_expenses(carrier_id: str, date: str):
    fuel_card = await db.get_carrier_fuel_card(carrier_id)
    
    if fuel_card.network == "comdata":
        transactions = await comdata_api.get_transactions(fuel_card.card_number, date)
    elif fuel_card.network == "efs":
        transactions = await efs_api.get_transactions(fuel_card.card_number, date)
    
    for txn in transactions:
        # Match to active load by timestamp and location
        load = await match_expense_to_load(txn["timestamp"], txn["location"], carrier_id)
        
        if load:
            await record_expense({
                "load_id": load.id,
                "carrier_id": carrier_id,
                "type": "FUEL",
                "amount": txn["amount"],
                "gallons": txn["gallons"],
                "price_per_gallon": txn["ppu"],
                "location": txn["location"],
                "timestamp": txn["timestamp"],
                "source": "fuel_card_auto",
            })
```

### Step 2 — Per-Load P&L Calculation

```python
async def calculate_load_profitability(load_id: str) -> dict:
    load = await db.get_load(load_id)
    expenses = await db.get_load_expenses(load_id)
    
    gross_revenue = load.agreed_rate + load.accessorials_collected
    
    # Carrier costs
    fuel_cost = sum(e["amount"] for e in expenses if e["type"] == "FUEL")
    toll_cost = sum(e["amount"] for e in expenses if e["type"] == "TOLL")
    other_costs = sum(e["amount"] for e in expenses if e["type"] not in ["FUEL", "TOLL"])
    
    total_carrier_cost = fuel_cost + toll_cost + other_costs
    
    # Dispatch fee
    dispatch_fee = load.dispatch_fee_amount
    
    # Net profit to carrier
    net_profit = gross_revenue - dispatch_fee - total_carrier_cost
    net_margin = net_profit / gross_revenue
    
    # Revenue per mile metrics
    cpm_gross = gross_revenue / load.loaded_miles
    cpm_net = net_profit / load.loaded_miles
    
    return {
        "load_id": load_id,
        "gross_revenue": gross_revenue,
        "total_expenses": total_carrier_cost,
        "dispatch_fee": dispatch_fee,
        "net_profit": net_profit,
        "net_margin_pct": round(net_margin * 100, 1),
        "cpm_gross": round(cpm_gross, 3),
        "cpm_net": round(cpm_net, 3),
        "expense_breakdown": {
            "fuel": fuel_cost,
            "tolls": toll_cost,
            "other": other_costs,
        },
    }
```

# SKILL: Tax Reporting & 1099 Generation
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Annual (January) + quarterly IFTA.
**Phase**: 18
**Priority**: HIGH

---

## Purpose

Automatically generate and file 1099-NEC forms for every carrier paid more than $600 in a calendar year, and produce IFTA fuel tax reports quarterly. Missing these deadlines = IRS penalties for the dispatch service.

---

## 1099-NEC Generation (Annual)

### Timeline
- **January 31**: Mail/email 1099s to carriers
- **January 31**: File with IRS (e-file deadline)

```python
async def generate_annual_1099s(tax_year: int):
    # Get all carriers paid >$600 this year
    qualifying_carriers = await db.query("""
        SELECT carrier_id, carrier_name, ein_or_ssn, address,
               SUM(settlement_amount) as total_paid
        FROM driver_settlements
        WHERE EXTRACT(YEAR FROM paid_at) = $1
        GROUP BY carrier_id, carrier_name, ein_or_ssn, address
        HAVING SUM(settlement_amount) >= 600
    """, tax_year)
    
    for carrier in qualifying_carriers:
        # Generate 1099-NEC
        form_data = {
            "payer_name": DISPATCH_SERVICE_NAME,
            "payer_ein": DISPATCH_SERVICE_EIN,
            "payer_address": DISPATCH_SERVICE_ADDRESS,
            "recipient_name": carrier["carrier_name"],
            "recipient_tin": carrier["ein_or_ssn"],  # EIN preferred; SSN masked
            "recipient_address": carrier["address"],
            "box1_nonemployee_compensation": carrier["total_paid"],
            "tax_year": tax_year,
        }
        
        # Generate PDF via Tax1099 API
        pdf = await tax1099_api.generate_1099_nec(form_data)
        
        # Store in S3
        s3_path = f"tax/{tax_year}/1099s/{carrier['carrier_id']}-1099.pdf"
        await s3.upload(s3_path, pdf)
        
        # Email to carrier
        await send_email(
            to=carrier["email"],
            subject=f"Your 1099-NEC for {tax_year} — [Dispatch Service Name]",
            body=f"""Hi {carrier['owner_name']},

Please find attached your 1099-NEC for {tax_year}.

Total nonemployee compensation: ${carrier['total_paid']:,.2f}

This form reports payments made by [Dispatch Service Name] to your business
for transportation services. Please retain this for your tax records.

If you have questions about the amount, please contact us.

[Dispatch Service Name]""",
            attachment=pdf,
        )
    
    # E-file with IRS via Tax1099
    await tax1099_api.efile_batch(qualifying_carriers, tax_year)
    
    return {"count": len(qualifying_carriers), "filed": True}
```

## IFTA Quarterly Reports

```python
async def generate_ifta_report(carrier_id: str, quarter: int, year: int):
    # Pull ELD mileage by state for the quarter
    eld_data = await eld_api.get_state_mileage(carrier_id, quarter, year)
    
    # Pull fuel purchases by state from fuel card data
    fuel_data = await fuel_card_api.get_purchases_by_state(carrier_id, quarter, year)
    
    # Build IFTA calculation
    states = set(list(eld_data.keys()) + list(fuel_data.keys()))
    
    ifta_summary = {}
    for state in states:
        miles = eld_data.get(state, 0)
        gallons_purchased = fuel_data.get(state, {}).get("gallons", 0)
        
        # Calculate fuel consumed in state (miles / mpg)
        mpg = await get_carrier_mpg(carrier_id)
        gallons_consumed = miles / mpg
        
        # Net fuel position
        net_gallons = gallons_consumed - gallons_purchased
        
        # Tax owed/refund
        ifta_rate = IFTA_RATES[state][quarter][year]
        tax_impact = net_gallons * ifta_rate
        
        ifta_summary[state] = {
            "miles": miles,
            "gallons_consumed": round(gallons_consumed, 2),
            "gallons_purchased": gallons_purchased,
            "net_gallons": round(net_gallons, 2),
            "tax_rate": ifta_rate,
            "tax_owed": round(tax_impact, 2) if tax_impact > 0 else 0,
            "refund_due": round(abs(tax_impact), 2) if tax_impact < 0 else 0,
        }
    
    total_owed = sum(s["tax_owed"] for s in ifta_summary.values())
    total_refund = sum(s["refund_due"] for s in ifta_summary.values())
    net_payment = total_owed - total_refund
    
    # Generate PDF report
    pdf = generate_ifta_pdf(carrier, ifta_summary, net_payment, quarter, year)
    
    return {"pdf": pdf, "net_payment": net_payment, "due_date": get_ifta_due_date(quarter, year)}
```

  - recommendations: "actions to improve cash position"

---

# SKILL: Cash Flow Forecasting
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Weekly Sunday evening.
**Phase**: 18
**Priority**: MEDIUM

---

## Purpose

Predict the next 30 days of cash inflows and outflows so the dispatch service never gets caught with insufficient funds to pay settlements or cover operating costs.

---

## Forecasting Model

```python
async def generate_weekly_forecast() -> dict:
    today = date.today()
    forecast_weeks = 4
    
    weekly_forecast = []
    
    for week in range(forecast_weeks):
        week_start = today + timedelta(weeks=week)
        week_end = week_start + timedelta(days=7)
        
        # Expected inflows
        dispatch_fees_due = await db.query("""
            SELECT SUM(fee_amount)
            FROM dispatch_fees
            WHERE expected_payment_date BETWEEN $1 AND $2
            AND status = 'INVOICED'
        """, week_start, week_end)
        
        # Expected outflows
        settlements_due = await db.query("""
            SELECT SUM(settlement_amount)
            FROM pending_settlements
            WHERE expected_payment_date BETWEEN $1 AND $2
        """, week_start, week_end)
        
        tech_costs = WEEKLY_TECH_COSTS  # ~$1,350/week at 50 carriers
        
        net_cash_flow = (dispatch_fees_due or 0) - (settlements_due or 0) - tech_costs
        
        weekly_forecast.append({
            "week": week_start.isoformat(),
            "dispatch_fees_expected": dispatch_fees_due or 0,
            "settlements_due": settlements_due or 0,
            "tech_costs": tech_costs,
            "net_cash_flow": net_cash_flow,
            "cumulative_position": sum(w["net_cash_flow"] for w in weekly_forecast) + net_cash_flow,
        })
    
    # Identify liquidity risks
    alerts = []
    for week in weekly_forecast:
        if week["cumulative_position"] < 5000:  # Below $5k buffer
            alerts.append({
                "week": week["week"],
                "severity": "WARNING" if week["cumulative_position"] > 0 else "CRITICAL",
                "message": f"Cash position drops to ${week['cumulative_position']:,.0f}",
                "recommendation": "Accelerate invoice collection or reduce advance issuance",
            })
    
    return {
        "generated_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "weekly_forecast": weekly_forecast,
        "alerts": alerts,
        "total_outstanding_receivables": await get_total_receivables(),
        "current_bank_balance": await get_bank_balance_from_qb(),
    }
```

# DOMAIN 5 - LEGAL, FRAUD & RISK (Skills X-BB)

---
skill_id: "X-double-brokering-fraud-detection"
name: "Double Brokering & Freight Fraud Detection"
version: "1.0.0"
phase: 6
priority: critical
trigger: "Before every load booking. Also triggered by unusual broker/carrier behavior patterns."
inputs:
  - broker_mc: "broker MC number"
  - carrier_mc: "carrier MC number"
  - load_details: "origin, destination, commodity, rate"
  - booking_context: "how load was found, broker history"
outputs:
  - fraud_risk_score: "0–100 (100 = definitely fraudulent)"
  - fraud_flags: "array of specific red flags identified"
  - recommendation: "BOOK | CAUTION | DO_NOT_BOOK"
  - evidence: "documentation of risk factors"
integrations:
  - Highway.com API (cargo theft & double-brokering database)
  - FMCSA SAFER API
  - DAT Broker Credit
  - TIA Watchlist API
  - TMS (historical patterns)
depends_on: ["06-load-triage-eligibility"]
triggers_next: ["10-load-booking (if safe to proceed)"]
tags: [fraud, double-brokering, cargo-theft, security, risk, compliance, fmcsa]
---

# SKILL: Double Brokering & Freight Fraud Detection
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Every load booking — non-negotiable check.
**Phase**: 6
**Priority**: CRITICAL — $700M+ lost annually to freight fraud

---

## Purpose

Detect double brokering, fake broker identities, MC number misuse, and cargo theft networks before booking. One fraudulent load can result in total cargo loss with no insurance recovery.

---

## Fraud Pattern Catalog

### Type 1 — Double Brokering
A load broker receives a load from a shipper, then re-brokers it to another carrier without the shipper's knowledge. The carrier gets paid (sometimes); the original broker disappears with the money.

**Red flags:**
- Broker's MC shows "freight broker" authority but they're posting as a carrier
- Rate offered is unusually high (trying to move load fast)
- Broker can't provide shipper name or contact
- Payment terms: "pay on delivery" (urgency to complete before victim realizes)
- MC number recently activated (<30 days)

### Type 2 — Identity Fraud
Scammer uses a legitimate carrier's MC number to steal a load.

**Red flags:**
- Phone number for "carrier" doesn't match FMCSA registration
- Email domain doesn't match registered business
- Carrier has no DOT inspection history (ghost company)
- Address on FMCSA doesn't match what they provide

### Type 3 — Fictitious Pickup / Phantom Load
Scammer posts fake loads on DAT/Truckstop to collect carrier packets and banking information.

**Red flags:**
- Load posts with no physical address — only "call for details"
- Rate is 30%+ above market for no clear reason
- Broker refuses to provide shipper name
- Demands W-9 and bank info before sending RC

---

## Fraud Detection Algorithm

```python
async def assess_fraud_risk(broker_mc: str, carrier_mc: str, load: dict) -> dict:
    risk_score = 0
    flags = []
    
    # ─── BROKER CHECKS ───
    
    # Highway.com database check
    highway_result = await highway_api.check_broker(broker_mc)
    if highway_result.get("double_brokering_reports") > 0:
        risk_score += 50
        flags.append(f"HIGHWAY_FLAG: {highway_result['double_brokering_reports']} double-brokering reports")
    
    if highway_result.get("cargo_theft_reports") > 0:
        risk_score += 60
        flags.append(f"CARGO_THEFT_HISTORY: {highway_result['cargo_theft_reports']} reports")
    
    # FMCSA authority check
    fmcsa = await fmcsa_api.lookup(broker_mc)
    
    if fmcsa.get("operating_status") != "ACTIVE":
        risk_score += 70
        flags.append(f"BROKER_NOT_ACTIVE: status={fmcsa.get('operating_status')}")
    
    mc_age_days = (date.today() - fmcsa.get("authority_granted_date", date.today())).days
    if mc_age_days < 30:
        risk_score += 30
        flags.append(f"NEW_MC_NUMBER: only {mc_age_days} days old")
    elif mc_age_days < 90:
        risk_score += 10
        flags.append(f"YOUNG_MC: {mc_age_days} days old")
    
    # DAT credit check
    dat_credit = await dat_api.get_broker_credit(broker_mc)
    if dat_credit.get("score", 100) < 40:
        risk_score += 30
        flags.append(f"LOW_DAT_CREDIT: score={dat_credit.get('score')}")
    
    # TIA watchlist
    tia_result = await tia_api.check(broker_mc)
    if tia_result.get("on_watchlist"):
        risk_score += 60
        flags.append(f"TIA_WATCHLIST: {tia_result.get('reason')}")
    
    # ─── LOAD PATTERN CHECKS ───
    
    # Rate anomaly detection
    market_rate = await dat_api.get_market_rate(load["origin"], load["destination"], load["equipment"])
    
    if load.get("posted_rate") and load["posted_rate"] > market_rate * 1.30:
        risk_score += 20
        flags.append(f"RATE_TOO_HIGH: ${load['posted_rate']:.2f} vs market ${market_rate:.2f}")
    
    # No shipper info provided
    if not load.get("shipper_name") and risk_score > 20:
        risk_score += 15
        flags.append("NO_SHIPPER_INFO: broker refuses to provide shipper details")
    
    # ─── CARRIER CHECKS (if verifying a carrier) ───
    if carrier_mc:
        carrier_fmcsa = await fmcsa_api.lookup(carrier_mc)
        
        if carrier_fmcsa.get("entity_type") == "BROKER":
            risk_score += 80
            flags.append("CARRIER_IS_BROKER: MC belongs to a broker, not a carrier — likely impersonation")
        
        highway_carrier = await highway_api.check_carrier(carrier_mc)
        if highway_carrier.get("theft_history"):
            risk_score += 70
            flags.append("CARRIER_THEFT_HISTORY: carrier has reported cargo theft incidents")
    
    # ─── FINAL RECOMMENDATION ───
    if risk_score >= 60:
        recommendation = "DO_NOT_BOOK"
    elif risk_score >= 30:
        recommendation = "CAUTION"
    else:
        recommendation = "BOOK"
    
    return {
        "broker_mc": broker_mc,
        "fraud_risk_score": min(risk_score, 100),
        "flags": flags,
        "recommendation": recommendation,
        "checked_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
    }
```

---

## Real-Time Alert Protocol

When `DO_NOT_BOOK` is returned:
1. Block the booking immediately
2. Log fraud attempt with full details
3. Add broker/carrier to internal blacklist
4. Report to DAT if DAT is involved
5. Alert human escalation if carrier is mid-load

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Highway API unavailable | Use FMCSA + DAT + TIA only; flag as partial check |
| MC number not found in any database | DO_NOT_BOOK — cannot verify |
| False positive (legitimate carrier flagged) | Human review; whitelist after verification |

skill_id: "Y-freight-claims-management"

  - evidence: "photos, BOL notations, weight tickets"
  - claimed_amount: "float — broker/shipper's stated loss"
outputs:

  - settlement_recommendation: "CONTEST | SETTLE | PAY"
  - filing_deadline_alert: "days remaining to respond"

# SKILL: Freight Claims Management
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Any cargo claim — damage, shortage, or loss.
**Phase**: 17
**Priority**: CRITICAL — missed claim deadlines = automatic loss of legal defense

---

## Purpose

Manage every cargo claim systematically. The Carmack Amendment gives shippers 9 months to file claims and carriers 30 days to acknowledge. Missing these deadlines surrenders all defenses.

---

## Statutory Deadlines (Carmack Amendment)

| Milestone | Deadline |
|-----------|----------|
| Carrier acknowledge claim | 30 days from receipt |
| Carrier pay, decline, or offer settlement | 120 days from acknowledgment |
| Claimant file lawsuit | 2 years from carrier denial |
| Carrier's claim against broker | 90 days (varies) |

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Claim Receipt and Logging

```python
async def open_freight_claim(claim_data: dict) -> dict:
    claim = {
        "claim_id": f"CLM-{generate_id()}",
        "load_id": claim_data["load_id"],
        "claim_type": claim_data["claim_type"],
        "reported_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "claimed_by": claim_data["reported_by"],
        "claimed_amount": claim_data["claimed_amount"],
        "evidence_urls": claim_data.get("evidence_urls", []),
        "status": "OPEN",
        
        # Set statutory deadlines
        "acknowledge_deadline": (datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=30)).isoformat(),
        "response_deadline": (datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=150)).isoformat(),
    }
    
    await db.insert("freight_claims", claim)
    
    # Immediately alert dispatcher
    await human_escalation.create(
        reason="FREIGHT_CLAIM_OPENED",
        context=claim,
        urgency="P1",
    )
    
    return claim
```

### Step 2 — Evidence Collection

```python
async def collect_claim_evidence(claim_id: str, load_id: str) -> dict:
    load = await db.get_load(load_id)
    
    evidence = {
        # Documentary evidence
        "rate_confirmation": load.rc_signed_url,
        "bill_of_lading": load.bol_url,
        "proof_of_delivery": load.pod_url,
        "call_recordings": await get_call_recordings(load_id),
        
        # GPS/Time evidence
        "geofence_timestamps": await get_geofence_data(load_id),
        "driver_check_calls": await get_check_call_log(load_id),
        
        # Physical evidence
        "delivery_photos": load.delivery_photos,
        "bol_exceptions_noted": load.bol_exceptions,
        
        # Weather/Force majeure
        "weather_events": await get_weather_events_for_route(load_id),
    }
    
    # Key defense: clean BOL = delivered in good order
    bol_data = await document_ocr.extract(load.bol_url, doc_type="BOL")
    evidence["clean_bol"] = not bol_data["fields"].get("exceptions_noted")
    evidence["receiver_signature_present"] = bool(bol_data["fields"].get("receiver_signature"))
    
    return evidence
```

### Step 3 — Claim Assessment

```python
def assess_claim_validity(claim: dict, evidence: dict) -> dict:
    recommendation = "CONTEST"
    defense_strength = 0
    defenses = []
    
    # Defense 1: Clean BOL (strongest defense)
    if evidence["clean_bol"] and evidence["receiver_signature_present"]:
        defense_strength += 40
        defenses.append("Clean BOL signed by receiver — goods delivered in good order")
    
    # Defense 2: No exception noted at delivery
    if not claim.get("exception_at_delivery"):
        defense_strength += 20
        defenses.append("No damage exception noted at time of delivery")
    
    # Defense 3: Shipper-packed cargo
    if claim["claim_type"] == "DAMAGE" and evidence.get("shipper_packed"):
        defense_strength += 25
        defenses.append("Shipper-packed — carrier not liable for internal packaging")
    
    # Defense 4: Acts of God / Force majeure
    if evidence.get("weather_events"):
        defense_strength += 15
        defenses.append(f"Weather event documented: {evidence['weather_events']}")
    
    # Assess settlement recommendation
    if defense_strength >= 60:
        recommendation = "CONTEST"
    elif defense_strength >= 30 and claim["claimed_amount"] > 500:
        recommendation = "NEGOTIATE"
    elif claim["claimed_amount"] < 200:
        recommendation = "SETTLE"  # Not worth contesting small claims
    
    return {
        "recommendation": recommendation,
        "defense_strength": defense_strength,
        "defenses": defenses,
    }
```

### Step 4 — Formal Response Letter

```python
def generate_claim_response(claim: dict, assessment: dict) -> str:
    if assessment["recommendation"] == "CONTEST":
        template = """
FORMAL CLAIM RESPONSE
Date: {date}
Re: Freight Claim #{claim_id} | Load {load_id}

Dear {claimant_name},

We acknowledge receipt of your claim dated {claim_date} for {claimed_amount} 
regarding the above-referenced shipment.

After thorough investigation of this claim, we respectfully DENY liability 
for the following reasons:

{defenses}

Supporting documentation attached:
- Signed Bill of Lading (no exceptions noted)
- Proof of Delivery
- GPS tracking records confirming route
{additional_docs}

This denial is issued pursuant to the Carmack Amendment (49 U.S.C. § 14706).
You have the right to file suit within two years of this denial.

[Dispatch Service Name]
        """
    elif assessment["recommendation"] == "SETTLE":
        template = """
CLAIM SETTLEMENT OFFER
[Settlement offer at or below claimed amount...]
        """
    
    return template.format(**claim, **assessment)
```

---

## Deadline Monitoring

```python
async def monitor_claim_deadlines():
    """Runs daily — alerts on approaching deadlines"""
    open_claims = await db.get_claims(status="OPEN")
    
    for claim in open_claims:
        days_to_acknowledge = (
            datetime.fromisoformat(claim["acknowledge_deadline"]) - datetime.utcnow()
        ).days
        
        if days_to_acknowledge <= 7:
            await human_escalation.create(
                reason="CLAIM_DEADLINE_APPROACHING",
                context={"claim_id": claim["id"], "days_remaining": days_to_acknowledge},
                urgency="P1",
            )
        elif days_to_acknowledge <= 0:
            await human_escalation.create(
                reason="CLAIM_DEADLINE_MISSED",
                urgency="P0",
            )
```

# SKILL: Cargo Theft Response
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: GPS goes dark or driver unreachable.
**Phase**: 13
**Priority**: CRITICAL — every minute matters in a cargo theft

---

## Purpose

Execute a structured, time-sensitive response when cargo theft is suspected or confirmed. Coordinate law enforcement, insurance, and recovery networks simultaneously.

---

## Theft Indicators

| Signal | Threshold | Action |
|--------|-----------|--------|
| GPS signal lost | >30 minutes | INVESTIGATE |
| Driver unresponsive | >2 hours | ESCALATE |
| Truck at unknown location (not route) | Any | INVESTIGATE |
| Theft explicitly reported | Immediate | FULL RESPONSE |
| Receiver reports no show | Immediate | INVESTIGATE |

---

## Response Timeline

### Minute 0-5 — Initial Alert

```python
async def initiate_theft_response(load_id: str, trigger: str):
    load = await db.get_load(load_id)
    
    # Attempt all driver contact methods simultaneously
    contact_attempts = await asyncio.gather(
        try_call_driver(load.driver_phone),
        try_whatsapp(load.driver_phone),
        try_call_owner(load.carrier_owner_phone),
        return_exceptions=True
    )
    
    any_response = any(r for r in contact_attempts if not isinstance(r, Exception))
    
    if not any_response:
        # Escalate to human and begin full response
        await human_escalation.create(
            reason="POTENTIAL_CARGO_THEFT",
            context={
                "load_id": load_id,
                "last_known_location": load.last_gps_location,
                "last_gps_timestamp": load.last_gps_timestamp,
                "trigger": trigger,
                "cargo_value": load.declared_value or "unknown",
                "commodity": load.commodity,
            },
            urgency="P0",
        )
```

### Minute 5-15 — Law Enforcement

If driver cannot be reached and location is suspicious:

```python
async def contact_law_enforcement(load: dict, last_location: dict):
    # Prepare incident report for police
    incident = {
        "vehicle_type": "Commercial Tractor-Trailer",
        "vehicle_description": f"{load.carrier.truck_year} {load.carrier.truck_make}",
        "license_plate": load.carrier.truck_plate,
        "vin": load.carrier.truck_vin,
        "trailer_number": load.carrier.trailer_number,
        "last_known_location": last_location,
        "cargo_description": load.commodity,
        "cargo_value_estimate": load.declared_value,
        "driver_name": load.driver_name,
        "driver_phone": load.driver_phone,
        "mc_number": load.carrier.mc_number,
    }
    
    # Alert dispatcher to call 911 (cannot auto-dial 911)
    await human_escalation.create(
        reason="CALL_911_CARGO_THEFT",
        context={
            "incident": incident,
            "nearest_law_enforcement": await get_nearest_law_enforcement(last_location),
            "instructions": "CALL 911 NOW. Provide VIN, plate, last location, cargo description.",
        },
        urgency="P0",
    )
    
    # Also alert state police via online portal
    state = get_state_from_location(last_location)
    await report_to_state_police_online(state, incident)
```

### Immediate — Industry Alert Networks

```python
async def alert_industry_networks(incident: dict):
    # CargoNet — largest cargo theft reporting network
    await cargonet_api.report_theft({
        "load_ref": incident["load_id"],
        "commodity": incident["commodity"],
        "last_location": incident["last_location"],
        "vehicle_info": incident["vehicle"],
        "driver_info": incident["driver"],
    })
    
    # FreightWatch International
    await freightwatch_api.create_alert(incident)
    
    # DAT — flag broker so they know load may not be delivered
    await dat_api.alert_broker(incident["broker_mc"], incident["load_ref"])
```

### Within 1 Hour — Insurance

```python
async def initiate_insurance_claim(load: dict, incident: dict):
    insurer = load.carrier.cargo_insurer
    
    # Notify insurance company immediately (most policies require prompt notice)
    await send_email(
        to=insurer.claims_email,
        subject=f"CARGO THEFT CLAIM — Policy #{load.carrier.cargo_policy_number}",
        body=f"""
This is immediate notice of a potential cargo theft incident.

Insured: {load.carrier.company_name}
Policy: {load.carrier.cargo_policy_number}
Date/Time: {incident['discovery_time']}
Location: {incident['last_known_location']}
Cargo: {load.commodity}
Estimated Value: ${load.declared_value:,.0f}
Load Reference: {load.broker_ref}

Law enforcement has been notified. Incident number: [pending]

Please contact us immediately at {DISPATCH_SERVICE_PHONE}.
        """,
    )
```

|-----------|--------|
| Driver was sleeping (false alarm) | Log false positive; update detection thresholds |
| GPS unit malfunction | Verify via cell triangulation; reduce false alarm priority |
| Police non-responsive | Escalate to FBI for high-value cargo (>$50K) |
| Insurance claim denied | Route to Y-freight-claims-management |

# SKILL: Service Agreement Generator
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Every new carrier onboarding.
**Phase**: 1
**Priority**: HIGH

---

## Purpose

Auto-generate a legally sound dispatch service agreement tailored to each carrier's fee structure and send it for e-signature. No agreement = no protection if carrier disputes fees or abandons a load.

---

## Agreement Template Sections

```python
SERVICE_AGREEMENT_SECTIONS = [
    "parties",                    # Legal names, MC numbers, addresses
    "services_provided",          # Full scope of dispatch services
    "dispatcher_fee_structure",   # Exact model, rate, billing cycle
    "carrier_obligations",        # Check-calls, HOS compliance, communication
    "payment_terms",              # When and how dispatcher collects fee
    "detention_policy",           # How detention is tracked and claimed
    "invoice_requirements",       # POD submission deadlines
    "termination_clause",         # 30-day notice, immediate for cause
    "dispute_resolution",         # Arbitration vs litigation, jurisdiction
    "liability_limitations",      # What dispatcher is/isn't liable for
    "confidentiality",            # Broker relationships, rate info
    "independent_contractor",     # Carrier is NOT an employee of dispatcher
    "power_of_attorney",         # Limited POA for paperwork submission
    "governing_law",              # Which state's law governs
    "entire_agreement",           # This supersedes all prior agreements
]
```

### Key Contract Terms

```python
async def generate_agreement(carrier: dict, fee_structure: dict) -> str:
    template = load_template("dispatch_service_agreement.html")
    
    # Calculate key dates
    effective_date = date.today()
    initial_term_end = effective_date + timedelta(days=30)  # 30-day initial
    
    context = {
        "carrier_legal_name": carrier["legal_name"],
        "carrier_dba": carrier.get("dba_name"),
        "carrier_mc": carrier["mc_number"],
        "carrier_dot": carrier["dot_number"],
        "carrier_address": carrier["address"],
        "carrier_owner_name": carrier["owner_name"],
        "carrier_state": carrier["state"],
        
        "dispatcher_name": DISPATCH_SERVICE_NAME,
        "dispatcher_ein": DISPATCH_SERVICE_EIN,
        "dispatcher_address": DISPATCH_SERVICE_ADDRESS,
        "dispatcher_state": DISPATCH_SERVICE_STATE,
        
        "fee_model": fee_structure["model"],
        "fee_rate": fee_structure["rate"],
        "fee_description": get_fee_description(fee_structure),
        
        "effective_date": effective_date.strftime("%B %d, %Y"),
        "initial_term": "30 days, then month-to-month",
        "termination_notice_days": 30,
        
        "detention_free_hours": 2,
        "detention_notice_requirement": "15 minutes before clock starts",
        
        "pod_submission_deadline_hours": 24,
        "invoice_submission_deadline_hours": 48,
        
        "governing_law_state": DISPATCH_SERVICE_STATE,
        "dispute_resolution": "binding arbitration (AAA rules)",
    }
    
    rendered_html = template.render(**context)
    
    # Convert to PDF
    pdf_bytes = html_to_pdf(rendered_html)
    
    # Upload to S3
    s3_path = f"carriers/{carrier['id']}/agreements/dispatch-agreement-{effective_date}.pdf"
    await s3.upload(s3_path, pdf_bytes)
    
    # Send for e-signature via DocuSign
    envelope = await docusign.create_envelope({
        "email_subject": "Please sign your Dispatch Service Agreement",
        "documents": [{"documentBase64": base64.b64encode(pdf_bytes).decode(), "name": "Dispatch Service Agreement"}],
        "signers": [{
            "name": carrier["owner_name"],
            "email": carrier["email"],
            "recipientId": "1",
            "tabs": {
                "signHereTabs": [{"anchorString": "CARRIER_SIGNATURE_HERE"}],
                "dateSignedTabs": [{"anchorString": "DATE_SIGNED_HERE"}],
            },
        }],
    })
    
    return {"envelope_id": envelope["envelopeId"], "s3_path": s3_path}
```

---
skill_id: "BB-data-privacy-compliance"
name: "Data Privacy & Compliance"
version: "1.0.0"
phase: 0
priority: medium
trigger: "Carrier offboarding request, data access request, or quarterly compliance review."
inputs:
  - request_type: "enum: DELETION | ACCESS | PORTABILITY | QUARTERLY_AUDIT"
  - carrier_id: "string (if carrier-specific)"
  - requestor: "carrier | regulator | internal"
outputs:
  - data_inventory: "all PII data held for this carrier"
  - deletion_confirmation: "all PII deleted if requested"
  - audit_report: "quarterly privacy compliance report"
integrations:
  - PostgreSQL (PII deletion)
  - AWS S3 (document deletion)
  - AWS KMS (encryption verification)
  - TMS

triggers_next: []

# SKILL: Data Privacy & Compliance
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Data rights requests + quarterly audits.
**Phase**: All
**Priority**: MEDIUM

---

## Purpose

Maintain GDPR/CCPA compliance for all carrier and driver PII. Fulfill data deletion requests within required timeframes. Prevent PII from leaking through logs, reports, or APIs.

---

## PII Inventory Per Carrier

```python
PII_FIELDS = {
    "carriers": ["owner_name", "home_address", "personal_email", "personal_phone"],
    "drivers": ["full_name", "ssn", "cdl_number", "home_address", "dob", "medical_cert_number"],
    "documents": ["W-9 (SSN)", "CDL copy", "bank_account_details"],
    "call_recordings": ["voice recording contains PII"],
    "messages": ["whatsapp chat history"],
}
```

### Deletion Workflow (Upon Offboarding Request)

```python
async def process_deletion_request(carrier_id: str) -> dict:
    """CCPA: Delete within 45 days. GDPR: Delete within 30 days."""
    
    deletion_log = []
    
    # 1. Database PII fields — overwrite with null or anonymized values
    await db.execute("""
        UPDATE carriers SET 
            owner_ssn = NULL,
            bank_routing = NULL,
            bank_account = NULL,
            home_address = '*** DELETED ***',
            personal_phone = NULL
        WHERE carrier_id = $1
    """, carrier_id)
    deletion_log.append("carrier PII anonymized in database")
    
    # 2. Delete documents from S3
    docs = await s3.list_objects(prefix=f"carriers/{carrier_id}/")
    for doc in docs:
        await s3.delete(doc.key)
    deletion_log.append(f"Deleted {len(docs)} documents from S3")
    
    # 3. Purge call recordings (retain if active dispute)
    recordings = await db.get_recordings(carrier_id)
    for rec in recordings:
        if not rec.get("dispute_hold"):
            await s3.delete(rec.s3_key)
    deletion_log.append(f"Deleted {len(recordings)} call recordings")
    
    # 4. WhatsApp message history
    await redis.delete(f"cortex:wa:context:{carrier.phone_number}")
    deletion_log.append("WhatsApp conversation history deleted")
    
    # 5. Mark carrier as DELETED in TMS (retain financial records for 7 years per IRS)
    await db.update_carrier(carrier_id, {
        "status": "DELETED",
        "deleted_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "deletion_type": "CARRIER_REQUEST",
    })
    deletion_log.append("Carrier marked DELETED (financial records retained per IRS)")
    
    return {
        "carrier_id": carrier_id,
        "deletion_completed_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "actions_taken": deletion_log,
        "financial_records_retained": True,  # Required by IRS for 7 years
    }
```

# SKILL: Carrier Prospecting & Recruitment
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Daily automated outreach campaign + manual trigger when truck inventory is low.  
**Phase**: 0 (Pre-Onboarding)  
**Priority**: MEDIUM  

---

## Purpose

Actively recruit new owner-operators and small fleets to expand the carrier base. A larger, quality carrier base means more truck options, better lane coverage, and less scrambling when a carrier is unavailable.

---

## Target Carrier Profile

**Ideal candidate:**
- Owner-operator or 1–5 truck fleet
- MC authority 90+ days old (some brokers require this)
- Safety rating: Satisfactory or None (no Conditional/Unsatisfactory)
- Clean CSA scores (no flagged BASICs)
- Equipment: 53' dry van, reefer, or flatbed (highest freight volume)
- Based in or running major freight lanes (Southeast, Midwest, Texas, California)

---

## Outreach Channels

### 1. Facebook Groups (Trucking Owner-Operator Communities)
- Search: "Owner Operators", "Truck Dispatchers", "Dry Van Freight", "Reefer Freight"
- Post in relevant groups:
  > "🚛 Looking for owner-operators and small fleets in [region]! We're a dispatch service that books loads, handles broker paperwork, rate negotiations, and invoicing — you just drive. No long-term contracts. Earning $[X]+ CPM on average. DM me or call [phone] to learn more."
- Respond to posts from drivers looking for loads or dispatchers

### 2. DAT / Truckstop Posted Trucks
- Search for trucks posted without a dispatcher in target lanes
- Call carriers directly: "Hi, I saw you have a truck posted in [city]. I'm a dispatcher — have you found your next load? I may have something for you."

### 3. LinkedIn (Fleet Owners and Operations Managers)
- Search: Owner-operator, Fleet Manager, Small Carrier
- Send connection request + brief intro message

### 4. Email/SMS Campaign (if carrier contact list available)
Template:
> Subject: Free yourself from the load board — we handle dispatch
> 
> Hi [Name],
> 
> Running your own truck is hard enough without spending 13 hours a week on load boards and broker calls. We're a full-service dispatch team that handles:
> • Finding and negotiating your loads on DAT/Truckstop
> • All broker paperwork (carrier packets, rate cons)
> • Invoicing and factoring coordination
> • 24/7 in-transit support
> 
> Our carriers average $X.XX+ CPM. No contracts. Pay only when you haul.
> 
> Interested? Let's talk: [phone] or reply to this email.
> 
> [Dispatcher Name]

### 5. Referral Program
- Active carriers refer other carriers → earn $[X] credit per successful referral

---

## Qualification Call (after carrier responds)

Questions to ask:
1. "What equipment do you run? How many trucks?"
2. "What's your MC authority date? How long have you been authorized?"
3. "What lanes do you prefer? Where are you based?"
4. "Are you currently working with a dispatcher? What's your biggest frustration?"
5. "What rate are you typically looking for per mile?"
6. "Do you use a factoring company? Which one?"
7. "Any special certifications — hazmat, TWIC, Oversize/OW?"

**Disqualify if:**
- MC authority inactive or <30 days old
- Safety rating Unsatisfactory
- Unwilling to sign dispatch agreement
- Using factoring company banned by major brokers

---

## CRM Tracking

Track each prospect in CRM:
- Contact info + equipment + lanes + rate expectations
- Date of first contact
- Follow-up schedule (3 touchpoints before marking cold)
- Status: `Prospect → Qualified → Onboarding → Active`

---

## Output
- Qualified prospects fed into `carrier-onboarding` skill ✅
- CRM updated with all prospect data ✅
- Weekly new carrier acquisition metric reported ✅


---

# SKILL: Carrier Onboarding
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: New carrier submits interest form OR dispatcher manually initiates onboarding for a prospect.  
**Phase**: 1 (Carrier Onboarding)  
**Priority**: CRITICAL  

---

## Purpose

Collect all required documents, verify legal compliance, and fully onboard a carrier into the dispatch system so they are ready to be assigned loads. A carrier cannot be dispatched until ALL required documents are verified and stored.

---

## Required Documents Checklist

| Document | Required | Notes |
|----------|----------|-------|
| MC/DOT Authority letter | ✅ Yes | Must be Active on FMCSA |
| W-9 (signed, current year) | ✅ Yes | Required for payment |
| Certificate of Insurance (COI) | ✅ Yes | See limits below |
| Notice of Assignment (NOA) / Factoring letter | If factored | Required if using factoring company |
| CDL copy (driver) | ✅ Yes | Must be valid, correct class |
| Truck registration | ✅ Yes | VIN, year, make, model |
| Trailer registration | If owned | VIN, year, type |
| Signed Dispatch Service Agreement | ✅ Yes | Before first load |
| Payment terms acknowledgement | ✅ Yes | Detention policy, invoice schedule |

### COI Minimum Requirements
- **Auto liability**: $1,000,000 minimum
- **Cargo insurance**: $100,000 minimum (reefer: $100,000 with reefer breakdown)
- **General liability**: $1,000,000 minimum
- **Endorsements**: Motor Truck Cargo, hired/non-owned auto
- Dispatch company MUST be listed as **Certificate Holder**

---

## Execution Steps

### Step 1 — Initial Contact
1. Send welcome email/SMS with secure document upload link
2. Include checklist of required documents
3. Set 48-hour deadline for document submission
4. Assign carrier a temp ID: `CARR-[MMYYYY]-[3-digit seq]`

### Step 2 — Document Collection
1. Monitor upload portal for incoming documents
2. Auto-acknowledge each document received
3. Check document quality (readable, complete, not expired)
4. Flag missing or low-quality documents immediately
5. Send reminder at 24 hours if incomplete

### Step 3 — FMCSA Verification (call FMCSA-VERIFICATION skill)
1. Look up MC number on FMCSA SAFER system: https://safer.fmcsa.dot.gov
2. Verify: Operating Status = ACTIVE
3. Verify: Authority type (Common/Contract/Broker)
4. Check MC age (days since operating authority granted)
5. Check safety rating (Satisfactory / None / Conditional — NOT Unsatisfactory)
6. Check CSA scores (BASICs violations, out-of-service rate)
7. Verify insurance filings on file with FMCSA

### Step 4 — Insurance Verification
1. Call insurance agent directly using phone on COI
2. Confirm policy is active and in force
3. Confirm coverage limits meet requirements
4. Request COI-on-demand email capability (for future broker requests)
5. Note policy expiration date — set 30-day renewal reminder

### Step 5 — Document Storage
1. Create carrier folder: `carriers/[MC#]/`
2. Store all documents with standardized file names:
   - `MC-Authority.pdf`
   - `W9-[Year].pdf`
   - `COI-[InsuranceCarrier]-[ExpDate].pdf`
   - `NOA-[FactoringCompany].pdf`
   - `CDL-[DriverLastName].pdf`
   - `TruckReg-[VIN].pdf`
   - `TrailerReg-[VIN].pdf`
   - `DispatchAgreement-Signed.pdf`
3. Log all expiration dates in compliance calendar

### Step 6 — Profile Creation
1. Create carrier record in TMS/CRM
2. Enter all basic info (MC#, DOT#, company name, owner name, phone, email)
3. Set insurance expiration alerts (30 days, 7 days, 1 day before)
4. Set CDL expiration alerts
5. Trigger `carrier-profile-management` skill to capture preferences

### Step 7 — Communication Setup
1. Confirm preferred communication channels (call/text/WhatsApp/email)
2. Set expected response time window (e.g., within 10 min during business hours)
3. Add driver and owner contact numbers separately
4. Set up dispatch notification preferences

### Step 8 — Welcome & Activation
1. Send welcome confirmation with:
   - Their assigned dispatcher contact
   - How to submit availability each day
   - How loads will be sent for approval
   - Payment timeline expectations
2. Mark carrier status: `ACTIVE`
3. Log activation date

---

## Outputs

- Carrier record created in TMS ✅
- All documents stored and indexed ✅
- Compliance calendar updated ✅
- FMCSA/insurance verified ✅
- Service agreement signed ✅
- Carrier marked ACTIVE ✅

---

## Integration Requirements

- **FMCSA SAFER API**: Real-time authority verification
- **Document OCR tool**: Auto-parse PDF fields (MC#, DOT#, expiry dates)
- **TMS/CRM**: Carrier record storage
- **Email/SMS gateway**: Welcome sequences, reminders
- **Cloud storage**: Document vault per carrier
- **Calendar/alert system**: Expiration reminders

---

## Error Handling

| Error | Action |
|-------|--------|
| MC authority Inactive/Revoked | Reject carrier — do NOT proceed. Notify and explain. |
| Safety rating Unsatisfactory | Reject carrier — do NOT proceed. |
| COI limits below minimum | Request updated COI before proceeding. |
| W-9 missing or unsigned | Cannot process payment — hold activation. |
| Factoring company on broker ban list | Notify carrier — may limit load options. |
| Document expired | Request renewal before activation. |

---

## Quality Gate

**DO NOT activate carrier until ALL of the following are confirmed:**
- [ ] MC Authority = ACTIVE on FMCSA
- [ ] Safety rating ≠ Unsatisfactory
- [ ] COI meets minimum limits
- [ ] All required documents received and readable
- [ ] Dispatch agreement signed
- [ ] W-9 on file


---
