# SKILL NN — Competitive Intelligence
================================================================================

---
skill_id: "NN-competitive-intelligence"
name: "Competitive Intelligence"
version: "1.0.0"
phase: 18
priority: medium
trigger: "Monthly automated competitive review. Also triggered when carrier mentions a competitor."
inputs:
  - competitor_mentions: "from carrier conversations — any mention of other dispatch services"
  - market_signals: "new entrants, pricing changes, feature announcements"
outputs:
  - competitive_landscape: "who is competing for our carriers and at what price/offering"
  - positioning_gaps: "where competitors are weak"
  - strategic_recommendations: "pricing, feature, or outreach adjustments"
integrations:
  - Web research (GPT-4o + web search)
  - CRM (carrier conversation logs)
  - TMS (carrier acceptance/rejection patterns)
depends_on: []
triggers_next: ["KK-dispatch-pricing-strategy", "LL-carrier-retention-churn"]
tags: [competitive, intelligence, market, positioning, pricing, benchmarking]
---

## Purpose

Stay informed about competing dispatch services, their pricing, and what they offer carriers. Use this intelligence to sharpen our pricing, improve our value proposition, and identify carriers at risk of being poached.

## Competitor Landscape (2026)

### Primary Competitors

| Competitor | Model | Pricing | Strength | Weakness |
|-----------|-------|---------|----------|---------|
| TruckSmarter | AI dispatch platform | 6–8% | Tech-forward, app-based | Less personal relationship |
| Bubba AI | AI voice calling | 5–7% | Strong voice AI | Newer, less proven |
| Numeo | AI dispatch | 5–6% | Low price | Limited support, thin team |
| Traditional dispatchers | Human dispatchers | 8–12% | Personal relationship | Expensive, 9-5 hours |
| Owner doing own dispatch | None | 0% | Free | 13+ hrs/week lost to dispatch work |

### Competitive Positioning Matrix

```
                HIGH PRICE
                    │
    Traditional ────┤──── (no one is here)
    Dispatchers     │
                    │
──────────────────────────────────────
MANUAL ◄────────────┼──────────────► AUTOMATED
                    │
    Cortex Bot ─────┤──── TruckSmarter
    (this system)   │    Bubba AI
                    │    Numeo
                LOW PRICE
```

**Goal**: Own the "Low Price + High Automation" quadrant.

## Intelligence Collection

### Source 1 — Carrier Conversation Mining (Automated)

```python
async def scan_for_competitor_mentions(carrier_id: str, conversation_history: List[str]):
    """Detect competitor mentions in WhatsApp/call transcripts."""
    
    COMPETITORS = [
        "trucksmarter", "truck smarter", "bubba", "numeo", 
        "dat dispatch", "convoy", "uber freight",
        # Generic signals
        "another dispatcher", "switching", "better deal", "cheaper"
    ]
    
    mentions = []
    for msg in conversation_history:
        for competitor in COMPETITORS:
            if competitor.lower() in msg.lower():
                mentions.append({
                    "carrier_id": carrier_id,
                    "mention": competitor,
                    "context": msg[:200],
                    "timestamp": datetime.utcnow()
                })
    
    if mentions:
        # Trigger churn risk elevation
        await update_churn_risk(carrier_id, boost=0.30)
        await alert_dispatcher(carrier_id, f"Competitor mention detected: {mentions}")
    
    return mentions
```

### Source 2 — Monthly Market Research (Automated)

```python
async def run_monthly_competitive_research():
    """Use web research to update competitive intelligence."""
    
    # Search for competitor news, pricing, feature updates
    research_prompts = [
        "TruckSmarter dispatch service pricing 2026 owner operator review",
        "Bubba AI truck dispatch pricing features 2026",
        "Numeo dispatch service owner operator review 2026",
        "truck dispatch service pricing comparison 2026",
        "best dispatch service owner operator 2026 Reddit"
    ]
    
    findings = []
    for query in research_prompts:
        results = await web_search(query)
        summary = await claude_sonnet.analyze(
            f"Summarize key competitive intelligence from these results: {results}. "
            f"Focus on: pricing, features, carrier satisfaction, market positioning."
        )
        findings.append(summary)
    
    return synthesize_competitive_report(findings)
```

### Source 3 — Lost Carrier Analysis

When a carrier leaves:
```python
async def run_exit_interview(carrier_id: str, churn_reason: str):
    """Extract maximum intelligence from every carrier departure."""
    
    exit_data = {
        "carrier_id": carrier_id,
        "last_revenue": get_carrier_revenue(carrier_id, last_90_days=True),
        "churn_reason": churn_reason,
        "destination": "competitor" if "competitor" in churn_reason else "unknown",
        "competitor_name": extract_competitor_name(churn_reason),
        "competitor_price": extract_competitor_price(churn_reason)
    }
    
    # Feed into pricing model
    if exit_data["competitor_price"]:
        await update_competitive_price_database(
            competitor=exit_data["competitor_name"],
            observed_price=exit_data["competitor_price"],
            date=date.today()
        )
    
    return exit_data
```

## Monthly Competitive Intelligence Report

```
COMPETITIVE INTELLIGENCE — March 2026

PRICING LANDSCAPE:
• TruckSmarter: 6–7% (unchanged from February)
• Bubba AI: 5% introductory → 6.5% after 60 days (new intel from carrier interview 3/15)
• Numeo: 5% flat (confirmed by 2 carriers this month)
• Our pricing: 6% standard, 5.5% for 7+ loads/week

MARKET SIGNALS:
• Bubba AI announced Series A funding ($12M) — likely to expand marketing
• 2 carriers mentioned TruckSmarter "better app" — investigate UI improvements
• 1 carrier left for Numeo citing 1% lower fee — margin-sensitive segment

POSITIONING OPPORTUNITIES:
1. Numeo's low price attracts carriers, but reviews cite poor support.
   → Opportunity: position our 24/7 human escalation as differentiation.
2. TruckSmarter strong on tech/app but carriers feel "impersonal."
   → Opportunity: emphasize personal dispatcher relationship + Cortex Bot backing.
3. No competitor offers driver advance/Comchek capability widely.
   → Opportunity: promote Skill S (driver advances) more aggressively in onboarding.

RECOMMENDED ACTIONS:
1. Maintain 6% pricing — matching Numeo's 5% not worth the margin hit
2. Add "same-day advance" to all carrier onboarding conversations as differentiator
3. Monitor Bubba AI closely as they scale — likely to compete more directly in Q3
```

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| Carrier exaggerates competitor offer to negotiate | "I can't verify that, but tell me what rate would make you want to stay" |
| Competitor launches major new feature | Assess: build similar, partner, or find alternative positioning |
| Market-wide price compression | Review cost structure; identify efficiency gains before cutting price |

# SKILL O: EDI Integration
## Cortex Bot — Truck Dispatch Automation

**Trigger**: Inbound EDI 204 load tender.
**Phase**: 9 (Load Booking equivalent)
**Priority**: HIGH

---

## Purpose

Direct EDI connections to large shippers and brokers. Bypasses load boards entirely — loads arrive directly in CortexBot, are automatically accepted or declined, dispatched, and invoiced. Unlocks dedicated freight at higher margins (no broker middleman).

---

## EDI Transaction Set

| Transaction | Direction | Purpose |
|------------|----------|---------|
| EDI 204 | Inbound | Load tender from shipper — creates new load opportunity |
| EDI 990 | Outbound | Accept (A) or decline (D) the tender |
| EDI 214 | Outbound | Shipment status updates at each milestone |
| EDI 210 | Outbound | Freight invoice after delivery |
| EDI 997 | Both | Functional acknowledgement |

---

## Auto-Accept Logic

```python
async def evaluate_edi_tender(edi_204: dict) -> str:
    load = parse_edi_204(edi_204)
    
    # Run standard eligibility check (Skill 06)
    eligible = await run_triage(load)
    
    # Find best available carrier for this lane
    carrier = await find_best_carrier(
        origin=load.origin,
        destination=load.destination,
        equipment=load.equipment,
        pickup_date=load.pickup_date
    )
    
    if eligible and carrier and load.rate >= carrier.rate_floor:
        await send_edi_990(edi_204["shipment_id"], "A")  # Accept
        await create_load_from_edi(edi_204, carrier)
        return "ACCEPTED"
    else:
        await send_edi_990(edi_204["shipment_id"], "D")  # Decline
        return "DECLINED"
```

---

## EDI 214 Status Mapping

```python
EDI_214_STATUS_CODES = {
    "DISPATCHED":  ("X3", "Shipment dispatched"),
    "ARRIVED_PU":  ("X1", "Arrived at pickup"),
    "LOADED":      ("AF", "Loaded — departed pickup"),
    "IN_TRANSIT":  ("I1", "In transit"),
    "ARRIVED_DEL": ("X6", "Arrived at delivery"),
    "DELIVERED":   ("D1", "Delivered"),
    "EXCEPTION":   ("A9", "Exception — see note"),
}
```

---

## Error Handling

| Situation | Action |
|-----------|--------|
| EDI parsing error | Send EDI 997 with error code; alert dispatcher |
| No carrier available | Decline tender; log missed opportunity in CRM |
| Rate below floor | Decline; note rate for shipper negotiation (Skill MM) |
| EDI system down | Process via email fallback; alert Skill E |
